         <p>
          The
          <b>
           Twelfth Doctor
          </b>
          emerged from
          <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
           his predecessor
          </a>
          's explosive
          <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">
           regeneration
          </a>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/Trenzalore" title="Trenzalore">
           Trenzalore
          </a>
          , being the product of "regeneration number thirteen." He was the first incarnation of the Doctor's second regeneration cycle, which had been bestowed upon him by the
          <a href="/wiki/Time_Lord" title="Time Lord">
           Time Lords
          </a>
          .
          <a href="/wiki/Clara_Oswald" title="Clara Oswald">
           Clara Oswald
          </a>
          , continuing her travels with him after he regenerated, served as his primary
          <a href="/wiki/Companion" title="Companion">
           companion
          </a>
          , and at times acted as his moral compass.
         </p>
         <p>
          Assured of the survival of
          <a href="/wiki/Gallifrey" title="Gallifrey">
           Gallifrey
          </a>
          , he was no longer chained down by his guilt. A darker character with a withdrawn and spiky attitude, he was less amiable and habitually questioned his own goodness. Although this incarnation was no stranger to kindness and humour, he often dispensed with niceties in a tense situation, becoming cold and calculative in critical moments that required sound judgment and the occasional application of sharp practice.
         </p>
         <p>
          However, because of his detachment from emotions, he could come off as unpleasant, fearsome, and ruthless. These qualities often terrified those who were around him, even his companions. He became harder to trust, and acknowledged his shift toward negative personality traits, feeling incensed and fearful at what he was changing into.
         </p>
         <p>
          Unlike his predecessor's adventures with Clara, this Doctor found more strain was being placed on their relationship; Clara was dating fellow
          <a href="/wiki/Coal_Hill_School" title="Coal Hill School">
           Coal Hill
          </a>
          teacher
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Danny Pink
          </a>
          , whom the Doctor mutually disliked.
         </p>
         <nav class="toc" id="toc">
          <div id="toctitle">

           </h2>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">
           Biography
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit Biography section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">
           Preparations
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit Preparations section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          During a visit to a
          <a href="/wiki/Meta-fiction_universe" title="Meta-fiction universe">
           parallel universe
          </a>
          where he was a fictional character in a television series, the
          <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
           Eleventh Doctor
          </a>
          told his portrayer,
          <a href="/wiki/Matt_Smith" title="Matt Smith">
           Matt Smith
          </a>
          , that
          <a href="/wiki/Peter_Capaldi" title="Peter Capaldi">
           Peter Capaldi
          </a>
          , whom he had previously rescued from a
          <a href="/wiki/Mandrel" title="Mandrel">
           Mandrel
          </a>
          , would be a good choice to play him on the show. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Girl_Who_Loved_Doctor_Who_(comic_story)" title="The Girl Who Loved Doctor Who (comic story)">
            The Girl Who Loved Doctor Who
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Post-regeneration">
           Post-regeneration
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit Post-regeneration section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140901173650/tardis/images/c/ce/Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelfth Doctor Post-Regeneration" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor Post-Regeneration.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140901173650/tardis/images/thumb/c/ce/Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg" height="111" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelfth Doctor Post-Regeneration" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor Post-Regeneration.jpg" height="111" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140901173650/tardis/images/thumb/c/ce/Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelfth_Doctor_Post-Regeneration.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            A befuddled Twelfth Doctor staring intensely at
            <a href="/wiki/Clara_Oswald" title="Clara Oswald">
             Clara Oswald
            </a>
            immediately after his thirteenth regeneration. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Time of the Doctor (TV story)">
              The Time of the Doctor
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          After fighting in the Siege of Trenzalore for 900 years, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tales_of_Trenzalore:_The_Eleventh_Doctor%27s_Last_Stand" title="Tales of Trenzalore: The Eleventh Doctor's Last Stand">
            Tales of Trenzalore: The Eleventh Doctor's Last Stand
           </a>
          </i>
          ), the
          <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
           Eleventh Doctor
          </a>
          , facing extermination from the
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
           Daleks
          </a>
          in his old age, was ready to accept that he had reached the end of his final life. Unable to accept his death,
          <a href="/wiki/Clara_Oswald" title="Clara Oswald">
           Clara Oswald
          </a>
          appealed to the
          <a href="/wiki/Time_Lord" title="Time Lord">
           Time Lords
          </a>
          to intervene and the Doctor received a new regeneration cycle. After using the energy from the regenerative reset that followed to destroy the Dalek mother ship, the Doctor, still dying from old age, returned to his TARDIS to undergo his thirteenth regeneration.
         </p>
         <p>
          Suddenly changing in a flash before Clara's eyes, the new Doctor voiced his surprise at having new kidneys. The TARDIS then began shaking violently, and the Doctor implied to have forgotten how to pilot his ship, much to a shocked Clara's dismay. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Time of the Doctor (TV story)">
            The Time of the Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Crashing in pre-historic Earth, the TARDIS was chased and subsequently swallowed by a female
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tyrannosaur" title="Tyrannosaur">
           tyrannosaur
          </a>
          ; when the Doctor brought the TARDIS to
          <a href="/wiki/1890s" title="1890s">
           1890s
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">
           London
          </a>
          , the dinosaur was accidentally brought along with it.
         </p>
         <p>
          After the TARDIS was spat out, the Doctor, in a severe bout of post-regenerative trauma, acted very wild and irrationally. He peeked out of the TARDIS door, shushed
          <a href="/wiki/Strax" title="Strax">
           Strax
          </a>
          , slammed the door shut momentarily, and then finally crept out of the TARDIS, trying to identify him as one of the Seven Dwarves. Unable to remember names or faces clearly, he sputtered at the sight of the
          <a href="/wiki/Paternoster_Gang" title="Paternoster Gang">
           Paternoster Gang
          </a>
          , before being joined by a frazzled and annoyed Clara, trying to keep some degree of control on his livid and maddened state.
         </p>
         <p>
          Though put to bed to stabilise, the Doctor soon awoke and, grabbing a piece of
          <a href="/wiki/Chalk" title="Chalk">
           chalk
          </a>
          , doodled strange equations all over the bedroom. Hearing the dinosaur in pain, the Doctor climbed out onto the rooftop and left on horseback when he saw the T-Rex was being burned to ashes. Deciding to investigate, but still suffering a degree of post-regenerative stress, the Doctor wandered the streets of London. Talking to a passing tramp, the Doctor examined his new facial features, taking particular note of his new eyebrows, as well as his new Scottish accent, before trading in his previous incarnation's favourite watch for the tramp's coat. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Deep_Breath_(TV_story)" title="Deep Breath (TV story)">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829002026/tardis/images/c/cb/Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve Clara Half-Face Man" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Clara Half-Face Man.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829002026/tardis/images/thumb/c/cb/Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg/180px-Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelve Clara Half-Face Man" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Clara Half-Face Man.jpg" height="102" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829002026/tardis/images/thumb/c/cb/Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg/180px-Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_Clara_Half-Face_Man.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor and Clara examine the dormant
            <a href="/wiki/Half-Face_Man" title="Half-Face Man">
             Half-Face Man
            </a>
            .  (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
              Deep Breath
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Seeing an ad in a newspaper placed by
          <a href="/wiki/The_Master#As_Missy" title="The Master">
           Missy
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven_(TV_story)" title="Death in Heaven (TV story)">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) which seemed to be a message from Clara, the Doctor infiltrated a suspicious restaurant, where he and Clara learned that time travelling
          <a href="/wiki/Clockwork_Droid" title="Clockwork Droid">
           Clockwork Droids
          </a>
          , under the leadership of the
          <a href="/wiki/Half-Face_Man" title="Half-Face Man">
           Half-Face Man
          </a>
          , had been harvesting humans to repair themselves and reach the Promised Land. Trying to speak on peaceful terms, the Doctor snapped the Control Node out of his illusion of the Promised Land by revealing the true state of his existence. Conflicted and unsure, the Half-Face Man fell out of his
          <a href="/wiki/Escape_pod" title="Escape pod">
           escape pod
          </a>
          , either jumping or having been pushed by the Doctor. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Deep_Breath_(TV_story)" title="Deep Breath (TV story)">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor briefly left Clara behind to redecorate the TARDIS console room and settle on a new outfit. Returning for Clara, the Doctor spoke of the suspicious way Clara had met him in his previous incarnation, only for Clara to likewise voice her uncertainty of the Doctor's identity and asked to be returned home. Attempting to return Clara home, the Doctor ended up in
          <a href="/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">
           Glasgow
          </a>
          by mistake. However, Clara decided to go out for coffee with the new Doctor after the Eleventh Doctor called her and encouraged her to help the Doctor through his regeneration. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Deep_Breath_(TV_story)" title="Deep Breath (TV story)">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Am_I_a_good_man.3F">
           Am I a good man?
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit Am I a good man? section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Leaving Clara behind in Glasgow to get coffee, the Doctor shared an adventure with a mutant called
          <a href="/wiki/78351_(Lights_Out)" title="78351 (Lights Out)">
           78351
          </a>
          during his quest for coffee. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Lights_Out_(short_story)" title="Lights Out (short story)">
            Lights Out
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Intending to return with the coffee, the Doctor saved a
          <a href="/wiki/Combined_Galactic_Resistance" title="Combined Galactic Resistance">
           Combined Galactic Resistance
          </a>
          fighter pilot named
          <a href="/wiki/Journey_Blue" title="Journey Blue">
           Journey Blue
          </a>
          from a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalek_Saucer" title="Dalek Saucer">
           Dalek Saucer
          </a>
          attack, though left
          <a href="/wiki/Kai_Blue" title="Kai Blue">
           her brother
          </a>
          behind in the explosion. After prompting her into asking nicely, the Doctor returned Journey to her command ship, the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Aristotle_(spaceship)" title="Aristotle (spaceship)">
            Aristotle
           </a>
          </i>
          , where Colonel
          <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Blue" title="Morgan Blue">
           Morgan Blue
          </a>
          introduced him to a
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
           Dalek
          </a>
          that had developed a fault and turned good.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140831050608/tardis/images/8/81/Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve listening to Rusty" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve listening to Rusty.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140831050608/tardis/images/thumb/8/81/Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg/180px-Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelve listening to Rusty" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve listening to Rusty.jpg" height="102" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140831050608/tardis/images/thumb/8/81/Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg/180px-Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_listening_to_Rusty.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor, shrunken down inside a
            <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
             Dalek
            </a>
            , learns why it turned good. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek_(TV_story)" title="Into the Dalek (TV story)">
              Into the Dalek
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Returning for Clara, three weeks later from her perspective, the Doctor asked her if she thought he was a good man, a question that Clara found herself unable to answer, and returned to base to help the Dalek. Joined by Journey and two other soldiers named
          <a href="/wiki/Gretchen_Carlisle" title="Gretchen Carlisle">
           Gretchen Carlisle
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Ross_(Into_the_Dalek)" title="Ross (Into the Dalek)">
           Ross
          </a>
          , the Doctor and Clara used a
          <a href="/wiki/Molecular_nanoscaler" title="Molecular nanoscaler">
           Molecular nanoscaler
          </a>
          to miniaturise themselves and enter the Dalek  whom the Doctor nicknamed "
          <a href="/wiki/Rusty" title="Rusty">
           Rusty
          </a>
          ". After losing Ross to the
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek_antibody" title="Dalek antibody">
           Dalek's antibodies
          </a>
          , the Doctor discovered a radiation leak from within the Dalek and learned that Rusty had turned good after seeing a star being born. Following the radiation, the Doctor discovered damage to Rusty's power source was slowly killing him, and repaired the damage with his
          <a href="/wiki/Sonic_screwdriver" title="Sonic screwdriver">
           sonic screwdriver
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          However, fixing Rusty's power core resulted in the malfunction that turned Rusty good to be reversed, with Rusty's destructive nature returning, and causing Rusty to go on a killing spree, as well as send a distress beacon to summon the Daleks to the rebels' base. After getting slapped and lectured by Clara for his apathy, the Doctor realised he could turn Rusty good again by reawakening his memory of the star being born.
         </p>
         <p>
          Instructing Clara to find a way to restore Rusty's memories of the star, the Doctor made his way to the
          <a href="/wiki/Kaled_mutant" title="Kaled mutant">
           Kaled mutant
          </a>
          within Rusty to mind linked with him, causing Rusty to see the Doctor's hatred of the Daleks and destroy the Daleks that had responded to his distress beacon. Leaving to continue his crusade against the Daleks, Rusty commented that Doctor would have made a good Dalek before both of them left. After declining Journey's request to travel with him and Clara, the Doctor returned Clara home, both still unsure if the Doctor was a good man, but with Clara convinced he was at least trying to be one. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek_(TV_story)" title="Into the Dalek (TV story)">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="New_adventures_with_Clara">
           New adventures with Clara
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit New adventures with Clara section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Spending some more time on his own, the Doctor became alerted to a creature that disguised itself as a motorway to consume planets into other dimensions. Summoning Clara to assist him, the Doctor was surprised when the creature disappeared, unaware that Clara had tricked the creature into consuming itself. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Road_Rage_(Twelfth_Doctor_comic_story)" title="Road Rage (Twelfth Doctor comic story)">
            Road Rage
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He and Clara then assisted the
          <a href="/wiki/Paternoster_Gang" title="Paternoster Gang">
           Paternoster Gang
          </a>
          in defeating the scheme of
          <a href="/wiki/Orestes_Milton" title="Orestes Milton">
           Orestes Milton
          </a>
          to weaponise people. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Silhouette_(novel)" title="Silhouette (novel)">
            Silhouette
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Deciding to give Clara the choice of their next destination, the Doctor took her to
          <a href="/wiki/Sherwood_Forest" title="Sherwood Forest">
           Sherwood Forest
          </a>
          to meet
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          , though the Doctor was sceptical of Robin's actual existence. He was proven wrong immediately on arrival when Robin shot his TARDIS with an arrow; however, he remained determined to prove Robin Hood and his
          <a href="/wiki/Merry_Men" title="Merry Men">
           Merry Men
          </a>
          were a fake.
         </p>
         <p>
          After participating in an
          <a href="/wiki/Archery" title="Archery">
           archery
          </a>
          contest for a golden arrow, the Doctor, Clara and Robin were caught by the
          <a href="/wiki/Sheriff_of_Nottingham" title="Sheriff of Nottingham">
           Sheriff of Nottingham
          </a>
          , who had allied with alien robots disguised as
          <a href="/wiki/Knight_(Robot_of_Sherwood)" title="Knight (Robot of Sherwood)">
           his knights
          </a>
          . Escaping, the Doctor found out that the robots were trying to reach
          <a href="/wiki/Nethersphere" title="Nethersphere">
           the Promised Land
          </a>
          , but lacked sufficient
          <a href="/wiki/Gold" title="Gold">
           gold
          </a>
          to repair their engine. Believing Robin was also a robot, the Doctor was captured by the Sheriff as Clara and Robin escaped through a window. Leading a revolution in the Sheriff's dungeon, the Doctor was informed by the Sheriff that Robin Hood was not a robot, just as Robin came to his rescue and defeated the Sheriff. Assisting Robin with Clara's help, the Doctor helped launch the golden arrow into the ship to allow it to escape velocity and explode harmlessly in space.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141017132919/tardis/images/c/c5/12_and_Robin.jpg">
           <img alt="12 and Robin" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="12_and_Robin.jpg" data-image-name="12 and Robin.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141017132919/tardis/images/thumb/c/c5/12_and_Robin.jpg/180px-12_and_Robin.jpg" height="93" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>

           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:12_and_Robin.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor finally acknowledges
            <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
             Robin Hood
            </a>
            as a genuine person, not a myth. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood_(TV_story)" title="Robot of Sherwood (TV story)">
              Robot of Sherwood
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Robin, having learned about the Doctor's story from Clara, noted that the two of them were not so different from each other. Both of them were people born into status and privilege, giving up both to live the life of an adventurer in order to fight injustice. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood_(TV_story)" title="Robot of Sherwood (TV story)">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara used a
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Goo_bomb?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Goo bomb (page does not exist)">
           goo bomb
          </a>
          to foil the Sibro's attempt to weaponise a Conlanian clock tower, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Chime_Time_(comic_story)" title="Chime Time (comic story)">
            Chime Time
           </a>
          </i>
          ) orchestrated a ceasefire in a war between anthropomorphic cats and dogs by allying them against an army of alien fleas that planned to attack every planet in the universe, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Once_Bitten_(comic_story)" title="Once Bitten (comic story)">
            Once Bitten
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and helped the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/World_Brain?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="World Brain (page does not exist)">
           World Brain
          </a>
          find a new way of life after crash landing on its factory planet. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Crash_Landing_(comic_story)" title="Crash Landing (comic story)">
            Crash Landing
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          While investigating corruption in a distant colony, the Doctor was briefly framed for various crimes and locked up in the colony's asteroid
          <a href="/wiki/The_Prison" title="The Prison">
           prison
          </a>
          until he exposed its darkest security measure. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Blood_Cell_(novel)" title="The Blood Cell (novel)">
            The Blood Cell
           </a>
          </i>
          ) The Doctor and Clara rescued the spaceship
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Genetrix" title="Genetrix">
            Genetrix
           </a>
          </i>
          from
          <a href="/wiki/Wispy" title="Wispy">
           Whispies
          </a>
          by using the ship's sifters to suck them up. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Sunset_Over_Venus_(short_story)" title="Sunset Over Venus (short story)">
            Sunset Over Venus
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Visiting the planet
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Hoopoe?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Hoopoe (page does not exist)">
           Hoopoe
          </a>
          , the Doctor acted as Clara's
          <a href="/wiki/Lawyer" title="Lawyer">
           lawyer
          </a>
          after she was arrested for walking on the ground by the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Court_of_Birds?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Court of Birds (page does not exist)">
           Court of Birds
          </a>
          . His attempt to convince them she and him weren't cats backfired when the owls accused them of being mice, but the Doctor had foreseen this and had recruited the native cats to attack the owls with makeshifts wings, but ensured that the wings were too difficult to use properly, rendering them useless in the cats' pursuit of the owls. As he left with Clara in the TARDIS, the Doctor rewarded the cats with a box of canned tuna.  (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Court_of_Birds_(comic_story)" title="The Court of Birds (comic story)">
            The Court of Birds
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140913225613/tardis/images/1/1a/Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg">
           <img alt="Listen (TV Story)" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg" data-image-name="Listen (TV Story).jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140913225613/tardis/images/thumb/1/1a/Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg/180px-Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg" height="100" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Listen (TV Story)" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg" data-image-name="Listen (TV Story).jpg" height="100" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140913225613/tardis/images/thumb/1/1a/Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg/180px-Listen_%28TV_Story%29.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Listen_(TV_Story).jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor meditating on top of the TARDIS. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Listen_(TV_story)" title="Listen (TV story)">
              Listen
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          During one of Clara's breaks from the TARDIS, the Doctor became obsessed with the idea that a creature designed to hide was following him around and that everyone was similarly being followed. Visiting Clara for help in finding the hiders, by using the TARDIS
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Telepathic_circuit" title="Telepathic circuit">
           telepathic circuits
          </a>
          to pilot into her past. However, Clara got distracted by a phone call from her date
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Danny Pink
          </a>
          and piloted them into his past instead, back when Danny was called Rupert as a child. Finding a
          <a href="/wiki/Figure_(Listen)" title="Figure (Listen)">
           figure
          </a>
          under Rupert's bed sheet, the Doctor had Clara and Rupert turn their backs to allow the being to walk out the room unobserved, leaving them unsure if it really was a creature or just another child playing a trick on Rupert.
         </p>
         <p>
          Returning Clara to her date with the adult Danny Pink, the Doctor continued to follow his theory by trying to use a trace of Clara left in the telepathic circuits, ending up at the
          <a href="/wiki/End_of_the_universe" title="End of the universe">
           end of the universe
          </a>
          where a time traveller named Colonel
          <a href="/wiki/Orson_Pink" title="Orson Pink">
           Orson Pink
          </a>
          , Danny's descendant, had been trapped for six months. Intrigued by how following Clara's timeline led him to Orson, the Doctor returned for Clara and had them wait at the end of the universe for the night, believing it to be the perfect time to find out if the hiders were real. Finding a chance to confront the creature outside the ship, the Doctor sent Clara into the TARDIS and seemed to get a look at what he's been chasing before the atmospheric shell broke and Orson had to rescue him. As the Doctor was knocked out, and the TARDIS seemed to be under attack, Clara used the telepathic circuits to fly the TARDIS away.
         </p>
         <p>
          Waking up to find Clara gone, the Doctor called out to her and inadvertently alerted
          <a href="/wiki/First_Doctor" title="First Doctor">
           his younger self
          </a>
          to Clara's presence. Before he could investigate, Clara re-entered the TARDIS and made him promise to leave and not find out where they had landed. Afterwards, the Doctor returned Orson and Clara to their own times and, satisfied by what he had learned, underlined the word "Listen" that the creature had written on his chalkboard. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Listen_(TV_story)" title="Listen (TV story)">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor planned to rendezvous with Clara at Coal Hill School, but instead arrived at a replica of the school on an
          <a href="/wiki/Unnamed_planet_(The_Monsters_of_Coal_Hill_School)" title="Unnamed planet (The Monsters of Coal Hill School)">
           unnamed planet
          </a>
          , where Clara and
          <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Delobel" title="Jeff Delobel">
           Jeff Delobel
          </a>
          , a French teacher, had been abducted by
          <a href="/wiki/Creature_(The_Monsters_of_Coal_Hill_School)" title="Creature (The Monsters of Coal Hill School)">
           primitive aliens
          </a>
          planning to infiltrate Earth via Coal Hill School. In order thwart the invasion, the Doctor told the aliens a tale of Earth's Guardian, informing them that he was the guardian, scaring the aliens off. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Monsters_of_Coal_Hill_School_(comic_story)" title="The Monsters of Coal Hill School (comic story)">
            The Monsters of Coal Hill School
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Resuming their travels, the Doctor and Clara helped stranded
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Seevith?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Seevith (page does not exist)">
           Seevith
          </a>
          launch their ship, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/More_Than_Meets_the_Eye_(comic_story)" title="More Than Meets the Eye (comic story)">
            More Than Meets the Eye
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and helped Professor
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Faster?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Faster (page does not exist)">
           Faster
          </a>
          end the
          <a href="/wiki/17th_century" title="17th century">
           17th century
          </a>
          witch trials. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Witch_Work_(comic_story)" title="Witch Work (comic story)">
            Witch Work
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Returning to pick up Clara, and persuade her to away from a date with Danny Pink in favour of other travel destinations, the Doctor received a call from Madame
          <a href="/wiki/Karabraxos" title="Karabraxos">
           Karabraxos
          </a>
          , who requested he free
          <a href="/wiki/The_Teller_(Time_Heist)" title="The Teller (Time Heist)">
           the Teller
          </a>
          and its mate from the
          <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_Karabraxos" title="Bank of Karabraxos">
           Bank of Karabraxos
          </a>
          , as he had done on the day she met him. Realising the ramifications of this request, the Doctor built up the identity of "the Architect", using this identity to stage a bank heist for him to commit, with the assistance of Clara, an
          <a href="/wiki/Augmented_human" title="Augmented human">
           augmented human
          </a>
          named
          <a href="/wiki/Psi" title="Psi">
           Psi
          </a>
          , and a shape shifting
          <a href="/wiki/Mutant_human" title="Mutant human">
           mutant human
          </a>
          named
          <a href="/wiki/Saibra" title="Saibra">
           Saibra
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Using
          <a href="/wiki/Memory_worm" title="Memory worm">
           memory worms
          </a>
          to erase the plan from their minds and prevent the Teller from alerting the young Karabraxos, the Doctor and Clara found themselves already in the Bank with their accomplices, their last memory being the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TARDIS_phone" title="TARDIS phone">
           TARDIS phone
          </a>
          ringing.
         </p>
         <p>
          Receiving instructions from the Architect on their location, objective, and the Bank's security system, the team infiltrated the Bank. Entering a safety deposit box, Team Not Dead - the Doctor's name for the assembled team - set of a
          <a href="/wiki/Dimensional_shift_bomb" title="Dimensional shift bomb">
           dimensional shift bomb
          </a>
          into a service corridor, where the team found a briefcase containing six teleporters disguised as
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Atomic_shredder?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Atomic shredder (page does not exist)">
           atomic shredders
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Seemingly losing Saibra and Psi to the shredders when the Teller locked onto them, the Doctor figured out that time travel was involved with the heist plan when a perfectly-timed
          <a href="/wiki/Solar_storm" title="Solar storm">
           solar storm
          </a>
          unlocked the Bank's vault. Retrieving what the Architect had promised Psi and Saibra as payment, the Doctor and Clara were caught by the Teller and delivered to the bank manager, Ms.
          <a href="/wiki/Delphox" title="Delphox">
           Delphox
          </a>
          . After Delphox left them to be executed, the Doctor and Clara were saved by Psi and Saibra, who revealed the true nature of the "shredders".
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140923003103/tardis/images/e/e6/Emboldened_Twelve.jpg">
           <img alt="Emboldened Twelve" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Emboldened_Twelve.jpg" data-image-name="Emboldened Twelve.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140923003103/tardis/images/thumb/e/e6/Emboldened_Twelve.jpg/180px-Emboldened_Twelve.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Emboldened Twelve" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Emboldened_Twelve.jpg" data-image-name="Emboldened Twelve.jpg" height="102" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140923003103/tardis/images/thumb/e/e6/Emboldened_Twelve.jpg/180px-Emboldened_Twelve.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Emboldened_Twelve.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor in a moment of elation after deducing himself as the Architect. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Time_Heist_(TV_story)" title="Time Heist (TV story)">
              Time Heist
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Venturing into the Bank's private vault to find his and Clara's reward, the Doctor instead found Director Karabraxos, and discovered that Delphox, as well as a majority of the bank's staff, was an exact clone of Karabraxos. Seeing Karabraxos' hatred of her own clones caused the Doctor to have an epiphany on the identity of the Architect, and he gave his phone number to Karabraxos as she fled from the solar storm about to hit the Bank. Subjecting himself to the Teller's powers, the Doctor regained his lost memories and realised the true objective of the bank heist. Freeing the Teller and its mate to a place to live in solitude, the Doctor then parted ways with Psi and Saibra, giving them their rewards, and returned Clara home for her date. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Time_Heist_(TV_story)" title="Time Heist (TV story)">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara were later pitted against the
          <a href="/wiki/Wyrrester" title="Wyrrester">
           Wyrresters
          </a>
          during their second attempt to invade Earth, with the Doctor also travelling back to ensure the failure of their first attempt and Clara briefly switching bodies with a Wyrrester before they were defeated. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Crawling_Terror_(novel)" title="The Crawling Terror (novel)">
            The Crawling Terror
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara were left to the mercy of
          <a href="/wiki/Sand_piranha" title="Sand piranha">
           sand piranhas
          </a>
          while chained to posts on a
          <a href="/wiki/Desert_planet" title="Desert planet">
           Desert planet
          </a>
          , rendezvoused with
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fish_Person" title="Fish Person">
           fish people
          </a>
          ,  (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Caretaker_(TV_story)" title="The Caretaker (TV story)">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) were saved from an
          <a href="/wiki/Aaraanandal_slime_beast" title="Aaraanandal slime beast">
           Aaraanandal slime beast
          </a>
          by a survivor of the
          <a href="/wiki/22nd_century_Dalek_invasion" title="22nd century Dalek invasion">
           22nd century Dalek invasion
          </a>
          named
          <a href="/wiki/Simon_(When_the_Wolves_Came)" title="Simon (When the Wolves Came)">
           Simon
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/When_the_Wolves_Came_(short_story)" title="When the Wolves Came (short story)">
            When the Wolves Came
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and outran soldiers to escape in the TARDIS. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Caretaker_(TV_story)" title="The Caretaker (TV story)">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) During
          <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">
           Christmas
          </a>
          , the Doctor and Clara saved a small village from a
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Cephla?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cephla (page does not exist)">
           Cephla
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Gift_Snatched!_(comic_story)" title="Gift Snatched! (comic story)">
            Gift Snatched!
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Planning to visit
          <a href="/wiki/Eden_2" title="Eden 2">
           Eden 2
          </a>
          , the Doctor was joined by a reluctant Clara, after she phoned him to drop her off at the school after she overslept. When the duo arrived, they found the under assimilation by the
          <a href="/wiki/Vladlack" title="Vladlack">
           Vladlack
          </a>
          , but it turned out that the planet was a trap, to lure in and arrest invaders of planets. Fearing that innocents could be inappropriately punished, the Doctor set up a warning beacon around the planet, then dropped Clara off at Coal Hill School. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Freeze_(comic_story)" title="Freeze (comic story)">
            Freeze
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Danny_and_Courtney">
           Meeting Danny and Courtney
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit Meeting Danny and Courtney section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Discovering a
          <a href="/wiki/Skovox_Blitzer" title="Skovox Blitzer">
           Skovox Blitzer
          </a>
          near
          <a href="/wiki/Coal_Hill_School" title="Coal Hill School">
           Coal Hill School
          </a>
          , the Doctor went in "deep cover" as the school's temporary caretaker to dispatch of the killer robot, much to Clara's dismay.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140930211201/tardis/images/0/06/Doctor_giving_commands_to_the_Skovox.jpg">
