           <noscript>
            <img alt="Doctor giving commands to the Skovox" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Doctor_giving_commands_to_the_Skovox.jpg" data-image-name="Doctor giving commands to the Skovox.jpg" height="102" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140930211201/tardis/images/thumb/0/06/Doctor_giving_commands_to_the_Skovox.jpg/180px-Doctor_giving_commands_to_the_Skovox.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Doctor_giving_commands_to_the_Skovox.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            An undercover Doctor dissuades a
            <a href="/wiki/Skovox_Blitzer" title="Skovox Blitzer">
             Skovox Blitzer
            </a>
            from using its
            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-destruct" title="Self-destruct">
             self-destruct
            </a>
            . (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/The_Caretaker_(TV_story)" title="The Caretaker (TV story)">
              The Caretaker
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Initially planning on using
          <a href="/wiki/Chronodyne_generator" title="Chronodyne generator">
           chronodyne generators
          </a>
          to send the Blitzer into the future, the Doctor's plan was accidentally foiled by
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Danny Pink
          </a>
          ; Danny had seen the Doctor act suspicuously and believed the devices were of malicious intent, deactivating some. As a result the Blitzer was sent a short time into the future, rather than centuries. After Clara introduced him as her boyfriend, the Doctor took a dislike to Danny as he was a former soldier and feared he wasn't good enough for Clara. He changed his plan to using a communication device to make the Blitzer think the Doctor was its superior.
         </p>
         <p>
          Rather a few days, the Blitzer returned during the next evening; to the Doctor's surprise, Danny used his military training to help keep the Blitzer occupied, allowing him to repair the malfunctioning device. After successfully commanding the Blitzer to deactivate with Danny's help, the Doctor took into space and ejected it from the TARDIS, taking Clara's troublesome pupil
          <a href="/wiki/Courtney_Woods" title="Courtney Woods">
           Courtney Woods
          </a>
          with him after she discovered his identity, deciding that there was no harm in having Courtney tag along as a travelling companion, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Caretaker_(TV_story)" title="The Caretaker (TV story)">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) but didn't see anything special in her. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon_(TV_story)" title="Kill the Moon (TV story)">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Further_adventures_with_Clara">
           Further adventures with Clara
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit Further adventures with Clara section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019220000/tardis/images/d/d2/TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg">
           <img alt="TITAN 12th 1 Run" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg" data-image-name="TITAN 12th 1 Run.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019220000/tardis/images/thumb/d/d2/TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg/180px-TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="TITAN 12th 1 Run" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg" data-image-name="TITAN 12th 1 Run.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019220000/tardis/images/thumb/d/d2/TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg/180px-TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TITAN_12th_1_Run.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Clara and the Doctor trying to escape as Rann-Korr reveals himself. (
            <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
             COMIC
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
              Terrorformer
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara travelled to the planet
          <a href="/wiki/Isen_VI" title="Isen VI">
           Isen VI
          </a>
          , so that Clara could practice skiing for a school trip. Although the Doctor remembered it as a very cold and snowy planet, it had been converted to a warm and tropical paradise. After rescuing Clara from monkey-like creatures, the Doctor found an artificial leaf, which led to him and Clara being accused of trespassing by the planet's owner,
          <a href="/wiki/Kano_Dollar" title="Kano Dollar">
           Kano Dollar
          </a>
          . The Doctor found that as a result of the planet's manipulation a global cataclysm was imminent, but Dollar wouldn't listen. The Doctor and Clara rescued two workers from an underground earthquake with the TARDIS and moved to a cavern beneath the tower. The Doctor had discovered a Gallifreyan signal and wanted to investigate. They found a giant terraformer, which had fused with a ship underground. From the ship came a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hyperion_(alien)" title="Hyperion (alien)">
           Hyperion
          </a>
          called
          <a href="/wiki/Rann-Korr" title="Rann-Korr">
           Rann-Korr
          </a>
          , who announced the universe would fall.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor released the ship's coolant gases, allowing him and the others to escape to the TARDIS. He explained that Rann-Korr's reanimation was a result of the terrorformer's work, and conceded he had no plan to defeat him. They returned to the surface and made plans with the workers. The Doctor returned to confront Rann-Korr in a last stand. As Rann-Korr prepared to kill the Doctor, the terrorformation was reverse-engineered, returning the area of Isen VI around him to its original icy state. The Doctor escaped in the TARDIS, and Rann-Korr was extinguished in the cold. He and Clara bid farewell to the workers and left. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
            Terrorformer
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          While Clara was having her
          <a href="/wiki/Mona_Lisa" title="Mona Lisa">
           portrait
          </a>
          painted by
          <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci" title="Leonardo da Vinci">
           Leonardo da Vinci
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/1505" title="1505">
           1505
          </a>
          , the Doctor received a summon to
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/2315?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2315 (page does not exist)">
           2315
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">
           India
          </a>
          from an old acquaintance of his, Tiger Maratha, who foresaw a timeless evil. The Doctor and Clara arrived in 2315 to find he had been killed and drained of life, and along with Tiger's daughter Priyanka were confronted by police who attempted to arrest the Doctor. Escaping capture, Priyanka told the Doctor and Clara that Tiger had worked for a group known as the Family Scindas. The Doctor, Clara and Priyanka travelled to the Scindas' ancestral home to find information, however the Doctor stumbled through a dimensional door into
          <a href="/wiki/1825" title="1825">
           1825
          </a>
          India, where he was attacked by a demon but rescued by renegade amazon Rani Jhulka. The Doctor and Rani found a necro-cloud harvesting the spirits of the dead, and then attacked by more of the demons. Before they could be overpowered by the demons, the TARDIS arrived, Priyanka having unintentionally activated the telepathic circuits. She told the Doctor Clara had been taken by the demons.
         </p>
         <p>
          Back in 2315, the Doctor, Priyanka and Rani found a final recorded message from Tiger made before his death, in which he explained he had collected three of the four mythic swords of the goddess Kali for the Family Scindas and had a premonition of evil over the swords. The Doctor was then summoned to see Chandra Scindas, the patriarch of the Scindas family. The Doctor deduced that they were beings known as the Kaliratha, putting themselves throughout time and space and Hindu mythology. Chandra revealed he had Clara hostage, ready to be burned by the Exodus rocket, forcing the Doctor to agree to find the fourth sword of Kali for them. The Doctor, Priyanka and Rani collected the fourth sword and returned to Chandra, who revealed he had used Clara as a host for the resurrection of Kali. Priyanka took control of the rocket while the Doctor battled with Kali. The Doctor revealed he hid his sonic screwdriver in the fourth sword, so that Kali unwittingly freed the evil spirits from her and released Clara's body, while Rani killed Chandra. The Doctor, Clara, Rani and Priyanka then attended a festival in Mumbai. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          While attempting to hang flowers on the exterior of the TARDIS, the Doctor was spooked by a future Clara and fell out of the TARDIS into the orbit of an asteroid. When Clara's attempt to avert the crisis ended up causing it, the TARDIS was able to save the Doctor by creating a time field around him. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/A_Long_Way_Down_(short_story)" title="A Long Way Down (short story)">
            A Long Way Down
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Picking up a signal, the TARDIS arrived on the
          <a href="/wiki/Quartz_Wastes" title="Quartz Wastes">
           Quartz Wastes
          </a>
          of
          <a href="/wiki/Asmoray" title="Asmoray">
           Asmoray
          </a>
          . Although the Doctor believed it was an uninhabited wasteland, Clara pointed out there was a harvester nearby extracting electricity from the quartz. The Doctor and Clara were brought aboard the harvester by two workers, where beings within the electricity had broken through and killed four workers. Their leader,
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Luther_(The_Body_Electric)?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luther (The Body Electric) (page does not exist)">
           Luther
          </a>
          , was insistent on continuing their work regardless. Investigating, the Doctor and Clara found the creatures were only attacking because they were being attacked - sucked into the harvester's storage batteries. With Clara's help, the Doctor was able to free the electricity beings back into the quartz. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Body_Electric_(comic_story)" title="The Body Electric (comic story)">
            The Body Electric
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Heading for Rome, the Doctor and Clara wound up in a Germanic forest, where they were apprehended and taken into a nearby encampment. There they learnt that robotic mosquitos were spreading disease and killing off dozens of soldiers. Tracking the energy fields of the mosquitos to a tower in the woods, the Doctor discovered the occupants were using the mosquitos to search for a cure to a plague infecting their own world. The Doctor convinced them to leave. Although Clara was worried about the rest of the sick soldiers, the Doctor told her to leave them, saying that everybody dies. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Silver_Mosquitos_(short_story)" title="Silver Mosquitos (short story)">
            Silver Mosquitos
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          After stopping a hostile invasion in the future, the Doctor travelled to
          <a href="/wiki/Tower_of_London" title="Tower of London">
           UNIT HQ
          </a>
          , where he had just been in time to shut down a
          <a href="/wiki/The_Void" title="The Void">
           Void
          </a>
          portal. The Doctor came into conflict with the Fractures, natives of the Void that possessed humans, who believed they had to drag anyone mark with
          <a href="/wiki/Void_stuff" title="Void stuff">
           Void stuff
          </a>
          into the Void to protect reality from unraveling. The chaos was started by a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNIT" title="UNIT">
           UNIT
          </a>
          scientist from an alternate Earth, Paul Foster, who wished to be with a version of his family. Recruiting UNIT,
          <a href="/wiki/Kate_Stewart" title="Kate Stewart">
           Kate Stewart
          </a>
          and the Fosters' help, the Doctor and Clara opened the Void, drawing the Fractures back inside and freeing their victims. At Clara's insistence, the Doctor allowed the alternate Paul to join his family in their universe, knowing the Fractures were entirely out for him now. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Fractures_(comic_story)" title="The Fractures (comic story)">
            The Fractures
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara travelled to the Sands Hotel in
          <a href="/wiki/1963" title="1963">
           1963
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas" title="Las Vegas">
           Las Vegas
          </a>
          after the Doctor found some tickets to see Frankie Seneca in a drawer. After proving to be a surprisingly good gambler, he caught the attention of Johnny Dragotta, who accused him of cheating. However, they were distracted when Mikey Nero, who was thought to have been killed, arrived, demanding control of the hotel. The Doctor unmasked Mikey as a disguised agent of the
          <a href="/wiki/Cybock_Imperium" title="Cybock Imperium">
           Cybock Imperium
          </a>
          , who began attacking the hotel. While trying to immoblise it, the Doctor was grabbed and throttled by the Imperium. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Gangland_(comic_story)" title="Gangland (comic story)">
            Gangland
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Fallout_with_Clara">
           Fallout with Clara
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit Fallout with Clara section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          At Clara's urging, the Doctor took her and Courtney to the Moon in
          <a href="/wiki/2049" title="2049">
           2049
          </a>
          , so that Courtney could be the first girl on the Moon to bolster her confidence. Landing instead in a recycled space shuttle heading for the moon, the Doctor was informed by Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Lundvik" title="Lundvik">
           Lundvik
          </a>
          that the moon had inexplicably gained mass, and that she and her crew were going to use nuclear bombs to dispose of the additional mass.
         </p>
         <p>
          Investigating a disused mining base from a previous mission, the Doctor, his companions and the astronauts found corpses preserved in webs and research that suggested that the moon was disintegrating. Soon after, the group was attacked by a spider creature, which Courtney killed with washing up equipment, but not before Lundvik's crew were killed.
         </p>
         <p>
          Taking a scared Courtney back to the TARDIS, the Doctor voiced his uncertainty of the Moon's fate to Clara, calling it a "gray area" in time. Exploring the moon's surface for the reason behind the deterioration, the Doctor, Clara and Lundvik discovered a horde of spider germs beneath the Moon's surface, as well as amniotic fluid, prompting the Doctor to investigate beneath the Moon for answers.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008010207/tardis/images/7/76/Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg">
           <img alt="Doctor Refusing to Interfere" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg" data-image-name="Doctor Refusing to Interfere.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008010207/tardis/images/thumb/7/76/Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg/180px-Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Doctor Refusing to Interfere" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg" data-image-name="Doctor Refusing to Interfere.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008010207/tardis/images/thumb/7/76/Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg/180px-Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Doctor_Refusing_to_Interfere.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor refuses to help humanity make a critical decision when time is in flux.  (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon_(TV_story)" title="Kill the Moon (TV story)">
              Kill the Moon
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Scanning the Moon's core, the Doctor discovered that the Moon was, in fact, an egg for an ancient creature that was hatching. Reuniting with Clara and Lundvik after the shuttle and the TARDIS fell into a canyon, the Doctor informed them of his discovery after establishing contact with Courtney's phone. While Clara and Lundvik argued about killing the creature for the sake of the Earth, the Doctor had Courtney bring the TARDIS to him via DVD, deciding that it was not his place to decide the Moon's future, and left in his TARDIS for Clara, Lundvik and Courtney to decide on behalf of humankind.
         </p>
         <p>
          After Clara chose to spare the creature, despite humanity voting for its death, the Doctor returned for the three women, taking them to a beach on Earth to see the creature hatch and the Moon harmlessly disintegrate in Earth's atmosphere. Confirming that the sight of the moon hatching kick started the humans pioneering into space, and seeing the creature hatch a new egg with same mass as the old Moon, the Doctor returned Courtney and Clara to Coal Hill School.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008012935/tardis/images/e/e6/Stunned_Twelve.jpg">
           <img alt="Stunned Twelve" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Stunned_Twelve.jpg" data-image-name="Stunned Twelve.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008012935/tardis/images/thumb/e/e6/Stunned_Twelve.jpg/180px-Stunned_Twelve.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Stunned Twelve" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Stunned_Twelve.jpg" data-image-name="Stunned Twelve.jpg" height="102" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141008012935/tardis/images/thumb/e/e6/Stunned_Twelve.jpg/180px-Stunned_Twelve.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Stunned_Twelve.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor looks on in stunned silence after Clara storms out of the TARDIS in disgust at his actions. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon_(TV_story)" title="Kill the Moon (TV story)">
              Kill the Moon
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          However, Clara, angered by the position the Doctor had put her in, asked the Doctor if he had known the egg was harmless, which the Doctor confirmed as true. Tired of the Doctor's apathy, Clara argued with the Doctor about how he had almost caused her to kill an unborn creature. He defended that he was helping the human race by not playing a part in this choice. However, Clara had been deeply hurt by the Doctor's constantly patronising attitude toward humanity, and now that he had demonstrated it with her, Clara felt reduced to the likes of an idiot in the Doctor's eyes. With tears rolling down her face, she told him to leave and not return for her. The Doctor was left stunned by her reaction and immediately took off. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon_(TV_story)" title="Kill the Moon (TV story)">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Time_alone">
           Time alone
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit Time alone section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Spending some time away from Clara, the Doctor joined a crew of six travellers, including a young
          <a href="/wiki/Geoffrey_Chaucer" title="Geoffrey Chaucer">
           Geoffrey Chaucer
          </a>
          , on a journey to the church at Santiago de	Compostela to avoid the plague. At the church, one of the travellers gave birth, then the group were attacked by life-feeding aliens disguised as wooden skeletons. However, the aliens recoiled in horror upon seeing the new baby. The Doctor realised the church was actually the aliens' disguised spaceship, and he and the crew escaped as the ship took off and away. The Doctor explained to Chaucer that the baby, representing new life, was enough to frighten away the death-conquering aliens. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Mercy_Seats_(short_story)" title="The Mercy Seats (short story)">
            The Mercy Seats
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Responding to a distress call from Dalek prisoner aboard a
          <a href="/wiki/Cyber_Ship" title="Cyber Ship">
           Cyber Ship
          </a>
          , the Doctor discovered that the Daleks,
          <a href="/wiki/Cyberman_(Mondas)" title="Cyberman (Mondas)">
           Cybermen
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Sontaran" title="Sontaran">
           Sontarans
          </a>
          were searching for the
          <a href="/wiki/Orb_of_Fates" title="Orb of Fates">
           Orb of Fates
          </a>
          to gain control of a powerful Time Lord weapon called the
          <a href="/wiki/Starbane" title="Starbane">
           Starbane
          </a>
          . The Doctor joined forces with the Dalek prisoner, who had been altered by the Cybermen and "seen the light" and nicknamed it "
          <a href="/wiki/Lumpy" title="Lumpy">
           Lumpy
          </a>
          ". Following the Orbs'
          <a href="/wiki/Artron_energy" title="Artron energy">
           Artron energy
          </a>
          to the
          <a href="/wiki/Cyber-tomb" title="Cyber-tomb">
           Cyber-tombs
          </a>
          of
          <a href="/wiki/Telos" title="Telos">
           Telos
          </a>
          , the Doctor restored a minimum of Lumpy's power, not trusting the Dalek to allow full use of its power, and sent him to retrieve the second Orb while he studied the first in the TARDIS.
         </p>
         <p>
          As Lumpy descended into the depths of Telos, the Doctor discovered that the Orbs were powered by temporal energy; The only way to destroy them was to create a temporal implosion. Leaving Telos for
          <a href="/wiki/Sontar" title="Sontar">
           Sontar
          </a>
          , the Doctor and Lumpy were trapped in a
          <a href="/wiki/Stasis_field" title="Stasis field">
           stasis field
          </a>
          by
          <a href="/wiki/Major" title="Major">
           Major
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Skar" title="Skar">
           Skar
          </a>
          , but the Doctor was able to open the field and allow Lumpy to escape undetected while he stayed behind as a diversion. After Lumpy acquired the last Orb and deactivated the stasis field, the Doctor escaped with Lumpy, deciding it best to stay clear of Sontar for a while. They next travelled to the Starbane. However,
          <a href="/wiki/Lumpy" title="Lumpy">
           Lumpy
          </a>
          pointed out that it was already occupied by
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
           Daleks
          </a>
          . When learning Lumpy was not turned to good, Doctor had found a way to access Lumpy's controls remotely and used this ability to destroy the
          <i>
           Starbane
          </i>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/GAME" title="GAME">
           GAME
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Doctor_and_the_Dalek" title="The Doctor and the Dalek">
            The Doctor and the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          On Christmas Eve 2014, the Doctor teamed up with
          <a href="/wiki/Ceri" title="Ceri">
           Ceri
          </a>
          , an understudy, to fraught an
          <a href="/wiki/Addos" title="Addos">
           Addos
          </a>
          attempt to recreate a
          <a href="/wiki/Mummers_play" title="Mummers play">
           Mummers play
          </a>
          by genetically altering actors from the
          <a href="/wiki/Palace_Theatre" title="Palace Theatre">
           Palace Theatre
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Behind_You_(short_story)" title="Behind You (short story)">
            Behind You
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor learnt that an invasion fleet of
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Megrati?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Megrati (page does not exist)">
           Megrati
          </a>
          were planning to attack the planet of
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Lemaria?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Lemaria (page does not exist)">
           Lemaria
          </a>
          , a plan he had previously stopped in his
          <a href="/wiki/First_Doctor" title="First Doctor">
           first incarnation
          </a>
          . The Doctor send them an invitation to give them some time to talk. While waiting for them to arrive, the Doctor took part in a Freedom Day celebratory play about the original defeat of the Lemaria, playing himself. The Doctor realised his
          <a href="/wiki/Fifth_Doctor" title="Fifth Doctor">
           fifth incarnation
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Adric" title="Adric">
           Adric
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Nyssa" title="Nyssa">
           Nyssa
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Tegan_Jovanka" title="Tegan Jovanka">
           Tegan Jovanka
          </a>
          were in the audience before the real Megrati arrived. As his past self and companions watched, the Doctor convinced the Megrati to leave the planet by threatening to destory their ships. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Constant_Doctor_(short_story)" title="The Constant Doctor (short story)">
            The Constant Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Clara_rejoins">
           Clara rejoins
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit Clara rejoins section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Reuniting with Clara for a farewell trip, the Doctor took her to a space-bound
          <a href="/wiki/Orient_Express_(spacecraft)" title="Orient Express (spacecraft)">
           Orient Express
          </a>
          . He later confessed to her that he had chosen the destination with an inkling that something exciting would happen after having been lured with
          <a href="/wiki/The_Big_Bang_(TV_story)" title="The Big Bang (TV story)">
           phone calls
          </a>
          , mysterious summons and free train tickets.
         </p>
         <p>
          After discovering the death of
          <a href="/wiki/Pitt_(Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express)" title="Pitt (Mummy on the Orient Express)">
           an elderly passenger
          </a>
          , and urging himself to investigate, the Doctor went to the engine room to examine the dead passenger's
          <a href="/wiki/Excelsior_Life_Extender" title="Excelsior Life Extender">
           Excelsior Life Extender
          </a>
          , meeting
          <a href="/wiki/Perkins_(Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express)" title="Perkins (Mummy on the Orient Express)">
           Chief Engineer Perkins
          </a>
          in the process, and learned the rumor of the
          <a href="/wiki/Foretold" title="Foretold">
           Foretold
          </a>
          . Seeking advice from
          <a href="/wiki/Emile_Moorhouse" title="Emile Moorhouse">
           Emile Moorhouse
          </a>
          , a fellow passenger who was a Professor of Alien Mythology, the Doctor soon discovered a second death had occurred in the kitchen.
         </p>
         <p>
          Confronting Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Quell" title="Quell">
           Quell
          </a>
          with his theory, but getting ignored, the Doctor joined Perkins and Moorhouse in the engine room to research the deaths. Calling Clara to update her, the Doctor discovered that she and
          <a href="/wiki/Maisie_Pitt" title="Maisie Pitt">
           Maisie Pitt
          </a>
          were trapped in a storage cart with a sarcophagus. Fearing that Clara was trapped with the Foretold, the Doctor tried to rewire the door open, only to find the sarcophagus empty, and himself under arrest by the Captain for being a stowaway.
         </p>
         <p>
          However, after witnessing a third death firsthand, Quell realised that the Doctor was right and allied with him, just as the Doctor deduced the true nature of the Orient Express; the passengers were all experts and scientists in specific fields of study, gathered there to study the Foretold. With a lab revealed and the hologram passengers disappearing, the train's computer,
          <a href="/wiki/Gus" title="Gus">
           Gus
          </a>
          , gave the scientists the necessary instructions and equipment. Losing Moorhouse to the Foretold, the Doctor and Perkins figured out that the Foretold was targeting the weaker passengers after looking at the medical history of the previous victims, just as Quell was killed by the creature, as he had
          <a href="/wiki/Post-traumatic_stress" title="Post-traumatic stress">
           post-traumatic stress
          </a>
          , but not before he gave the Doctor the necessary description to defeat the Foretold.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019003204/tardis/images/b/bc/Foretold_Approaches_Twelve.jpg">
           <img alt="Foretold Approaches Twelve" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Foretold_Approaches_Twelve.jpg" data-image-name="Foretold Approaches Twelve.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019003204/tardis/images/thumb/b/bc/Foretold_Approaches_Twelve.jpg/180px-Foretold_Approaches_Twelve.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>

           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Foretold_Approaches_Twelve.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor lets the
            <a href="/wiki/Foretold" title="Foretold">
             Foretold
            </a>
            prey on him, hoping to learn how it can be vanquished. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>

            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express_(TV_story)" title="Mummy on the Orient Express (TV story)">

             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Realising that Maisie was next due to her breakdowns, the Doctor told a reluctant Clara to bring Maisie to the lab. Arriving there, the Foretold appeared to Maisie, but the Doctor saved her by implanted a replica of her grief into his head, confusing the Foretold into thinking the Doctor was Maisie. Deducing that the Foretold was an ancient soldier augmented with technology, the Doctor surrendered, and, after a final salute, the ancient soldier crumpled to dust, with only the technology that kept him alive remaining.
         </p>
         <p>
          With the objective completed, Gus released the air out of the cabin, but the Doctor beamed all the dying passengers into the TARDIS, and tired to hack Gus to find out who had created him, but this trigged a security measure, causing the train to self-destruct. Dropping everyone but Clara and Perkins off at the nearest civilised planet, the Doctor waited for Clara to awaken on a beach before explaining everything.
         </p>
         <p>
          Back in the TARDIS, the Doctor invited Perkins to travel with him, but Perkins politely declined and he and the Doctor bade each other goodbye. Reflecting on a conversation she had with Maisie, Clara, having forgiven the Doctor, decided to continue travelling with him, telling the Doctor that her leaving was all Danny's idea. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express_(TV_story)" title="Mummy on the Orient Express (TV story)">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140928105017/tardis/images/d/dd/The_Eye_of_Torment.jpg">
           <img alt="The Eye of Torment" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="The_Eye_of_Torment.jpg" data-image-name="The Eye of Torment.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140928105017/tardis/images/thumb/d/dd/The_Eye_of_Torment.jpg/180px-The_Eye_of_Torment.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>

          </a>

           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:The_Eye_of_Torment.jpg">

             <i>

           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The Doctor landed on the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Pollyanna" title="Pollyanna">
            Pollyanna
           </a>
          </i>
          , the first of the
          <a href="/wiki/Ninth_Era" title="Ninth Era">
           Ninth Era
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Sunship" title="Sunship">
           sunships
          </a>
          , which had been on an expedition to circumnavigate
          <a href="/wiki/Sol" title="Sol">
           the Sun
          </a>
          . Seeing one of the
          <a href="/wiki/Umbra_(The_Eye_of_Torment)" title="Umbra (The Eye of Torment)">
           Umbra
          </a>
          come out of the Sun and enter a
          <a href="/wiki/Plasma_intake" title="Plasma intake">
           plasma intake
          </a>
          , the Doctor rushed to the
          <a href="/wiki/Plasma_lab" title="Plasma lab">
           plasma lab
          </a>
          and carried the injured
          <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">
           Professor
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Alice_Dubrovnik" title="Alice Dubrovnik">
           Alice Dubrovnik
          </a>
          to safety. The Umbra, who had been trapped in the
          <a href="/wiki/Chromosphere" title="Chromosphere">
           chromosphere
          </a>
          for millions of years, began swarming the
          <i>
           Pollyanna
          </i>
          , anchoring the ship to the Sun to try and hijack it and use it as a way of reaching Earth. As the Umbra on board took on more humans as vehicles, the Doctor was ejected out of a plasma intake to attract the Umbra to his regret. He set up the final link to Alice's
          <a href="/wiki/Graviton_inverter" title="Graviton inverter">
           graviton inverter
          </a>
          on the hull of the ship, allowing Alice to briefly boost the inverter and create a secondary
          <a href="/wiki/Gravity" title="Gravity">
           gravity
          </a>
          envelope, which inverted the gravity and the heat, freezing the Umbra on the ship to death. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Eye_of_Torment_(comic_story)" title="The Eye of Torment (comic story)">
            The Eye of Torment
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Trying to return Clara home, the Doctor instead landed in
          <a href="/wiki/Bristol" title="Bristol">
           Bristol
          </a>
          when the
          <a href="/wiki/Boneless" title="Boneless">
           Boneless
          </a>
          began draining power from the TARDIS, drawing it off course and causing the exterior to shrink. Sending Clara to find the cause, the Doctor re-entered the TARDIS to study the shrinking effect, only for the TARDIS to shrink further, trapping him inside. Equipping Clara with his
          <a href="/wiki/Psychic_paper" title="Psychic paper">
           psychic paper
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Sonic_screwdriver" title="Sonic screwdriver">
           sonic screwdriver
          </a>
          , the Doctor used nanotechnology to hack into Clara's optic nerve and establish a visual contact with the outer world. After Clara recruited the aid of a local named
          <a href="/wiki/Rigsy" title="Rigsy">
           Rigsy
          </a>
          , pretending to be the Doctor while doing so, the duo discovered that creatures from a two-dimensional universe were killing and dissecting missing locals to understand their three-dimensional bodies.
         </p>
         <p>
          After discovering that Clara had lied to him about Danny's approval, the Doctor realised that a mural dedicated to local missing people was in fact the missing people, killed and worn by the creatures as camouflage. With Clara leading a gang of surviving community servers, the Doctor theorised that the creatures were trying to communicate, and that the deaths were but a mere misunderstanding. When the theory was proved wrong, the Doctor invented a
          <a href="/wiki/2Dis" title="2Dis">
           2Dis
          </a>
           a device that could reverse the creatures' flattening abilities  as Clara and her gang retreated to an underground tunnel.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019043604/tardis/images/9/9a/Twelve_Tiny_TARDIS_Railroad_Track_Peril.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve Tiny TARDIS Railroad Track Peril" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_Tiny_TARDIS_Railroad_Track_Peril.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Tiny TARDIS Railroad Track Peril.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141019043604/tardis/images/thumb/9/9a/Twelve_Tiny_TARDIS_Railroad_Track_Peril.jpg/180px-Twelve_Tiny_TARDIS_Railroad_Track_Peril.jpg" height="97" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>

           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_Tiny_TARDIS_Railroad_Track_Peril.jpg">

            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">

            </a>

            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Flatline_(TV_story)" title="Flatline (TV story)">

             </a>
