           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          After Clara accidentally dropped the TARDIS onto a train line, the Doctor activated the TARDIS'
          <a href="/wiki/Siege_mode" title="Siege mode">
           siege mode
          </a>
          to protect it from an oncoming train. Now unable to even open the doors, which had been removed by the activation of siege mode, and with the life support systems failing as the power drain continued, the Doctor congratulated Clara for being worthy of the title Doctor, unsure if she could hear him or even if she was still alive. Clara and Rigsy were able to trick the creatures into supplying the TARDIS with the necessary power to restore it to full working conditions. Naming his adversaries the Boneless, and declaring himself as "The man that stops the monsters." the Doctor banished them back to their home universe. The Doctor then took the survivors to the surface. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Flatline_(TV_story)" title="Flatline (TV story)">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor tried taking Clara to the
          <a href="/wiki/Frost_fair" title="Frost fair">
           frost fair
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/1641" title="1641">
           1641
          </a>
          , but instead, was drawn off course and landed in the
          <a href="/wiki/Sahara_Desert" title="Sahara Desert">
           Sahara Desert
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/1941" title="1941">
           1941
          </a>
          , where they were captured by
          <a href="/wiki/Nazi" title="Nazi">
           Nazis
          </a>
          . While requesting business with Field Marshall
          <a href="/wiki/Erwin_Rommel" title="Erwin Rommel">
           Rommel
          </a>
          , the Doctor learnt from Rommel that
          <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">
           Germany
          </a>
          's allies, the
          <a href="/wiki/Tuareg" title="Tuareg">
           Tuareg
          </a>
          tribesmen, had made new extraterrestrial allies. The Doctor believed it was urgent to see the Tuareg and went with Rommel to meet them. After being taken to the tribe's chieftain,
          <a href="/wiki/Bhaki" title="Bhaki">
           Bhaki
          </a>
          , to see these "men from the stars" Bhaki introduced the Doctor and Rommel to the Tuareg's new allies, the
          <a href="/wiki/Sontaran" title="Sontaran">
           Sontarans
          </a>
          . The Sontaran
          <a href="/wiki/Commander" title="Commander">
           commander
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Kygon_Brox" title="Kygon Brox">
           Kygon Brox
          </a>
          , believing the Doctor was looking for the Sontaran world engine weapon, the
          <a href="/wiki/Warsong" title="Warsong">
           Warsong
          </a>
          , tried interrogating the Doctor with a
          <a href="/wiki/Mind_scythe" title="Mind scythe">
           mind scythe
          </a>
          . The Doctor made the link go the other way, and Kygon explained the history of the weapon to the Doctor. He told the Doctor that the Warsong was taken to Earth, and that there was someone seeking the weapon after signals from it began increasing exponentially. The Doctor realised that the "highly decorated" Nazi officer
          <a href="/wiki/Heinz_Bruckner" title="Heinz Bruckner">
           Heinz Bruckner
          </a>
          wasn't who he claimed he was, but a
          <a href="/wiki/Rutan_Host" title="Rutan Host">
           Rutan
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Spy" title="Spy">
           spy
          </a>
          and watched from a distance as the Warsong was triggered.
         </p>
         <p>
          Realising that Bruckner took Clara with him to the Warsong's activation, the Doctor came up with a plan to converge the
          <a href="/wiki/Allies" title="Allies">
           Allied
          </a>
          , Axis and Sontaran forces towards the still-forming Warsong to distract Bruckner while he and Rommel snuck into the Warsong and broke through its defences. The Doctor stopped Bruckner from conducting the milennia-old preset programming of the Warsong by using a Sontaran
          <a href="/wiki/Osmic_projector" title="Osmic projector">
           osmic projector
          </a>
          to send Bruckner's trigger mechanism through time. Rommel threw Bruckner into the Warsong, killing him, while the Doctor destroyed the "orchestra" of the Warsong by using his sonic screwdriver to blow it up. Afterwards, he brought Clara to the frost fair. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Instruments_of_War_(comic_story)" title="The Instruments of War (comic story)">
            The Instruments of War
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          After spending some time on his own, the Doctor landed in London, only to find it and the rest of the world overrun by trees after
          <a href="/wiki/Maebh_Arden" title="Maebh Arden">
           Maebh Arden
          </a>
          , a student of
          <a href="/wiki/Coal_Hill_Year_8_Gifted_and_Talented_Group" title="Coal Hill Year 8 Gifted and Talented Group">
           Coal Hill Year 8 Gifted and Talented Group
          </a>
          under Clara and Danny's care, looked for the Doctor after hearing about him in what Maebh believed was a thought that came from Clara. With his theories constantly being proven wrong, the Doctor came to the conclusion that the trees' sudden overgrowth was an act of aggression, while also dealing with Clara's students in his TARDIS after Clara and Danny arrived to collect Maebh, only for Maebh to slip away in the commotion, just as the Doctor noticed her homework had predicted the events of that day.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141107020512/tardis/images/3/3f/Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve Talks to Trees" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Talks to Trees.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141107020512/tardis/images/thumb/3/3f/Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg/180px-Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelve Talks to Trees" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Talks to Trees.jpg" height="102" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141107020512/tardis/images/thumb/3/3f/Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg/180px-Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_Talks_to_Trees.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor evokes the appearance of plant entities with his sonic screwdriver. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night_(TV_story)" title="In the Forest of the Night (TV story)">
              In the Forest of the Night
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Following Maebh deeper into the forest, the Doctor discovered that a sentience identifying itself as "the life that prevail[ed]" had caused the overgrowth, in preparation for a devastating
          <a href="/wiki/Solar_flare" title="Solar flare">
           solar flare
          </a>
          about to hit the Earth. Believing Earth doomed, Clara inquired him to use the TARDIS as a lifeboat, only to inform him that she had said that to get him back to his TARDIS so he could survive the catastrophe alone. Despite some reluctance, Clara eventually convinced him to leave. Immediately afterwards, having discovered upon further reflection that the trees were going to absorb the harmful solar flares by pumping the
          <a href="/wiki/Atmosphere" title="Atmosphere">
           atmosphere
          </a>
          with excess
          <a href="/wiki/Oxygen" title="Oxygen">
           oxygen
          </a>
          , "like a massive, highly inflammable
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Airbag?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Airbag (page does not exist)">
           airbag
          </a>
          ", the Doctor returned to Clara and explained his discovery to the Gifted and Talented Group.
         </p>
         <p>
          When he was informed of a government operation aiming to destroy the trees, the Doctor opened every mobile network on the planet to allow Maebh the opportunity to deliver a speech written by the Gifted and Talented Group to leave the trees alone. With Danny taking the children to their homes, the Doctor and Clara watched the trees that grown around the world harvesting and extinguishing the solar fire in the TARDIS, and then returned to watch the trees disappear on Clara's balcony. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night_(TV_story)" title="In the Forest of the Night (TV story)">
            In the Forest of the Night
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="The_darkest_hour">
           The darkest hour
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit The darkest hour section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          The Doctor rejoined Clara for a trip, where she suggested they go see a
          <a href="/wiki/Volcano" title="Volcano">
           volcano
          </a>
          . As the Doctor set the TARDIS to go, Clara attempted to put a
          <a href="/wiki/Mood_drug" title="Mood drug">
           mood patch
          </a>
          on his neck, but the Doctor realised what she was doing and turned it on her. Not realizing she was drugged, Clara imagined being at the volcano and throwing all the Doctor's TARDIS keys into lava, to blackmail him to save Danny, who had been killed in a road accident. The Doctor refused, and Clara came out of her dream state after destroying all the TARDIS keys. Despite her betrayal, the Doctor agreed to search for an afterlife to find Danny.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara arrived at
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/3W" title="3W">
           3W
          </a>
          , which held dead bodies in water tanks. They were greeted by
          <a href="/wiki/The_Master#As_Missy" title="The Master">
           Missy
          </a>
          , who identified herself as a greeting droid and kissed the Doctor as part of her greeting routine. They met
          <a href="/wiki/Chang_(Dark_Water)" title="Chang (Dark Water)">
           Dr. Chang
          </a>
          , who showed them the use of
          <a href="/wiki/Dark_water" title="Dark water">
           dark water
          </a>
          in the mausoleum. Clara received a call from Danny, who was in the
          <a href="/wiki/Nethersphere" title="Nethersphere">
           Nethersphere
          </a>
          , and the Doctor and Chang left her to take it.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141109204010/tardis/images/9/99/TwelveShockedDW.jpg">
           <img alt="TwelveShockedDW" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TwelveShockedDW.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveShockedDW.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141109204010/tardis/images/thumb/9/99/TwelveShockedDW.jpg/180px-TwelveShockedDW.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="TwelveShockedDW" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TwelveShockedDW.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveShockedDW.jpg" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141109204010/tardis/images/thumb/9/99/TwelveShockedDW.jpg/180px-TwelveShockedDW.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TwelveShockedDW.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor is horrified to realise his
            <a href="/wiki/The_Master" title="The Master">
             worst enemy
            </a>
            has returned. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
              Dark Water
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Chang discovered that the water tanks that held the bodies were being drained by Missy, who killed Chang and revealed that all the tanks held
          <a href="/wiki/Cyberman_(Mondas)" title="Cyberman (Mondas)">
           Cybermen
          </a>
          , who were preparing to invade Earth. Escaping the building, which he discovered
          <a href="/wiki/St_Paul%27s_Cathedral" title="St Paul's Cathedral">
           St Paul's Cathedral
          </a>
          , the Doctor tried to warn away nearby people, but Missy called out his warnings as insanity, and told him it was too late. The Doctor asked for her identity, and, to his shock, Missy revealed she was
          <a href="/wiki/The_Master#As_Missy" title="The Master">
           theMaster
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ) before she and the Doctor were apprehended by
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNIT" title="UNIT">
           UNIT
          </a>
          and brought aboard the plane
          <a href="/wiki/Boat_One" title="Boat One">
           Boat One
          </a>
          , where the Doctor was made President of Earth to battle the Cybermen. Missy overpowered UNIT, killed Osgood, and attempted to kill the Doctor by blowing up the plane, but the Doctor survived his fall to Earth by skydiving into the TARDIS. He travelled to a cemetery and reunited with Clara, who was comforting a converted Danny. Missy arrived and, as a "birthday present", gave the Doctor control of all the Cybermen.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093140/tardis/images/7/72/TwelveSalutes.jpg">
           <img alt="TwelveSalutes" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TwelveSalutes.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveSalutes.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093140/tardis/images/thumb/7/72/TwelveSalutes.jpg/180px-TwelveSalutes.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="TwelveSalutes" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TwelveSalutes.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveSalutes.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093140/tardis/images/thumb/7/72/TwelveSalutes.jpg/180px-TwelveSalutes.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TwelveSalutes.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor finally gives his
            <a href="/wiki/Alistair_Gordon_Lethbridge-Stewart" title="Alistair Gordon Lethbridge-Stewart">
             old friend
            </a>
            the salute he always wanted. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven_(TV_story)" title="Death in Heaven (TV story)">
              Death in Heaven
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Missy planned to turn the Doctor into the leader of the new army, intending to prove that the two of them were not that different after all, believing that she had put him in the impossible position of either accepting control of the army and using it to 'save' the universe or letting humanity die and conquer the universe as the Cybermen. However, reflecting on his past, the Doctor realised that he was just a man in a box who travelled around to help where he could, proclaiming that he was not a good man, a bad man, the leader of an army or a President. He then turned command of the army over to Danny, realizing that the teacher had held on to his love for Clara even with his emotions deactivated, who led the Cybermen into the clouds where they self-destructed and stopped the rainfall from converting the living. A devastated Missy told the Doctor he could find
          <a href="/wiki/Gallifrey" title="Gallifrey">
           Gallifrey
          </a>
          in its original location with coordinates she provided, but Clara threatened to kill Missy for what she had done, until the Doctor prepared to do it himself. However, a rogue Cyberman disintegrated Missy instead. The Doctor realised it was his old friend
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Brigadier" title="The Brigadier">
           the Brigadier
          </a>
           resurrected as a Cyberman  helping him again. The Doctor saluted the Brigadier, fulfilling a life-long wish of his old friend, noting that the Brigadier would never be anywhere else but by his side when Earth and the Doctor faced their darkest hour.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093225/tardis/images/5/5d/TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg">
           <img alt="TwelveClaraGoodbye" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093225/tardis/images/thumb/5/5d/TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg/180px-TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="TwelveClaraGoodbye" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" data-image-name="TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141111093225/tardis/images/thumb/5/5d/TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg/180px-TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TwelveClaraGoodbye.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor and Clara part ways. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven_(TV_story)" title="Death in Heaven (TV story)">
              Death in Heaven
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The Doctor entered the coordinates Missy gave him into the TARDIS and looked at his location, expecting to find Gallifrey. However, it turned out the coordinates were false and led to nowhere. With his only way to find Gallifrey gone, the Doctor attacked the TARDIS console in a furious rage, before breaking down emotionally. Meeting up with Clara in a caf, and believing that she was back with Danny, the Doctor lied to her that he had found Gallifrey so as to allow her to continue with her life. Upon hearing this, Clara told him that she was happy and ready to settle down with, and they both bid farewell and parted ways. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven_(TV_story)" title="Death in Heaven (TV story)">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Dreaming_of_Santa">
           Dreaming of Santa
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit Dreaming of Santa section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Some time later, the Doctor was attacked by a
          <a href="/wiki/Dream_crab" title="Dream crab">
           dream crab
          </a>
          , which put him into a scenario where he was brooding alone in his drifting TARDIS, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and was snapped out of his funk as when he heard
          <a href="/wiki/Santa_Claus" title="Santa Claus">
           Santa Claus
          </a>
          knocking on the TARDIS door, asking the Doctor what he wanted for Christmas. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven_(TV_story)" title="Death in Heaven (TV story)">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor travelled to Clara's home and collected her from her rooftop, where she had also encountered Santa. Urging her to believe in him, they arrived at a North Pole base, which they found was under attack from dream crabs. Santa arrived to help with the problem, but Clara was attacked by a crab and fell into a dream state. As no one could find a way to remove the crab from her face, the Doctor let himself be attacked by one to get her out of her dream before the crab could kill her.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141226064318/tardis/images/9/98/Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve Pulling Santa&#039;s Sleigh" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Pulling Santa's Sleigh.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141226064318/tardis/images/thumb/9/98/Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg/180px-Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelve Pulling Santa&#039;s Sleigh" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Pulling Santa's Sleigh.jpg" height="102" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141226064318/tardis/images/thumb/9/98/Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg/180px-Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_Pulling_Santa%27s_Sleigh.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Fleeing a dream world, an ecstatic Doctor gets to pull
            <a href="/wiki/Santa_Claus" title="Santa Claus">
             Santa
            </a>
            's sleigh. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
              Last Christmas
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Entering Clara's dream, the Doctor found she was dreaming of spending Christmas with Danny, and learned that Danny was dead. The Doctor urged her to break out of the dream, after Danny bid her farewell. Waking up in the base, the Doctor came to the realisation that everyone in the base was dreaming, having been attacked by crabs after they arrived. They woke up from the dream and the Doctor and Clara prepared to leave, but Clara reminded the Doctor of Santa having been on her roof, and he realised they were still dreaming from different places and times. The infected personnel in the base began to attack the survivors, however, everyone managed to escape by dreaming Santa was flying them home. The Doctor, Clara and the base scientists flew over London as they each woke up back in their own times.
         </p>
         <p>
          Waking up where he had been, the Doctor travelled to Clara's home and removed the dream crab attached to her, only to find it had been sixty-two years since he left her and she was now an old woman. Clara filled her in on the years, but the Doctor felt remorseful of leaving her when he did. Santa suddenly appeared and asked the Doctor what he'd do if he had another chance, and the Doctor woke up from his dream, this time for real. He saved the younger Clara from the crab. Spurred on by what could have happened to her, the Doctor invited her to resume her travels with him, and she accepted. They set off together in the TARDIS, the Doctor remarking that he rarely got second chances with his companions, and commenting that he didn't know who to thank for this one. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Second_chance_with_Clara">
           Second chance with Clara
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit Second chance with Clara section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Discovering that a group of aliens were going to turn a planet of anthropomorphic pink hippopotami into stone, the Doctor intercepted the aliens at the early stages of their invasion and led them to ancient
          <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">
           Egypt
          </a>
          , where they petrified a large cat-like alien, creating the
          <a href="/wiki/Sphinx" title="Sphinx">
           Sphinx
          </a>
          and getting crushed in the process. He and Clara then returned to the planet of the anthropomorphic pink hippopotamuses to reverse the petrified effect. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Petrified_(DWA_comic_story)" title="Petrified (DWA comic story)">
            Petrified
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara turned Captain
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Ratlett?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ratlett (page does not exist)">
           Ratlett
          </a>
          's crew against him and showed them a better life,  (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Wheelers_(comic_story)" title="The Wheelers (comic story)">
            The Wheelers
           </a>
          </i>
          ) were almost consumed by robotic bananas for stealing food from the
          <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">
           moon
          </a>
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Luna_Schlosser?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luna Schlosser (page does not exist)">
           Luna Schlosser
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Five_a_Day_(comic_story)" title="Five a Day (comic story)">
            Five a Day
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and saved the Cloud City of
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Mirmi_24?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mirmi 24 (page does not exist)">
           Mirmi 24
          </a>
          from being eaten by an alien snake. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Very_Hungry_Snake_(comic_story)" title="The Very Hungry Snake (comic story)">
            The Very Hungry Snake
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor attempted to take Clara to
          <a href="/wiki/Blackpool" title="Blackpool">
           Blackpool
          </a>
          , but they ended up arriving in
          <a href="/wiki/2089" title="2089">
           2089
          </a>
          , by which point the pleasure beach had become an overgrown jungle. The Doctor befriended and named
          <a href="/wiki/Meghan_(All_the_Empty_Towers)" title="Meghan (All the Empty Towers)">
           Meghan
          </a>
          , a wounded donkey shot by a man called
          <a href="/wiki/Triss_(All_the_Empty_Towers)" title="Triss (All the Empty Towers)">
           Triss
          </a>
          , who was planning a hunting trip in hover pods powered by the Blackpool Tower. The Doctor shut down the power, ending Triss' hunting plans. The Doctor and Clara had a dance in a ballroom, and then he enjoyed a play in the water with Meghan. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/All_the_Empty_Towers_(short_story)" title="All the Empty Towers (short story)">
            All the Empty Towers
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara travelled to a galactic
          <a href="/wiki/Auction" title="Auction">
           auction
          </a>
          in Earth's orbit where unclaimed storage was being bidded on, with the storage pod belonging to
          <a href="/wiki/Hyphen_T_Hyphen" title="Hyphen T Hyphen">
           Hyphen T Hyphen
          </a>
          , a reclusive collector, containing a mother
          <a href="/wiki/Rigellan_Hyper-Kraken" title="Rigellan Hyper-Kraken">
           Rigellan Hyper-Kraken
          </a>
          , which began killing everyone when the pod was opened. Before the mother Hyper-Kraken's eggs could hatch, the Doctor widened the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Dimensional_shunt?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dimensional shunt (page does not exist)">
           dimensional shunt
          </a>
          's focus on the Hyper-Kraken, her eggs and the storage pods and safely transported them elsewhere. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Space_Invaders!_(comic_story)" title="Space Invaders! (comic story)">
            Space Invaders!
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Taking Clara to the
          <a href="/wiki/Taj_Mahal" title="Taj Mahal">
           Taj Mahal
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">
           India
          </a>
          for a holiday, the Doctor was chosen to act as a hostage by
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Stellar_Nexus?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Stellar Nexus (page does not exist)">
           Stellar Nexus
          </a>
          while Nexus tried to get payment for Earth's supposed tax bills. When the Doctor challenged Nexus's claim by pointing out the illogic in his statement, and then insulted him by asking why he had never heard of Nexus's Empire, the Doctor was locked in a cell while an illusion of him was set against a dragon in a gladiator battle. When Clara managed to pilot the TARDIS into the Doctor's cell, the Doctor used his sonic screwdriver to deactivate Nexus's illusions, exposing that Stellar Nexus was a child-sized con artist whose entire Empire was an illusion. Sending the defeated Nexus away, the Doctor decided to treat Clara to a
          <a href="/wiki/Curry" title="Curry">
           curry
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Empire%27s_Fall_(comic_story)" title="Empire's Fall (comic story)">
            Empire's Fall
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor took Clara to see the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Lights_of_Tanzarr?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Lights of Tanzarr (page does not exist)">
           Lights of Tanzarr
          </a>
          , but instead found that the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Nameless_Mist?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nameless Mist (page does not exist)">
           Nameless Mist
          </a>
          had entered his dimension and was threatening to devour the cosmos. Originally wanting to flee, the Doctor was convinced by Clara to save the inhabitants of
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Ferrous-Ferra?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ferrous-Ferra (page does not exist)">
           Ferrous-Ferra
          </a>
          , and was inspired to recruit
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Cold_Steel?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cold Steel (page does not exist)">
           Cold Steel
          </a>
          to headline the "loudest rock show in history of sound". While Clara triangulated the transmissions to cover the local galaxy, the Doctor used the loud music to thwart off the Nameless Mist. With the day saved, the Doctor returned to the concert to celebrate with crowd surfing. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Big_Hush_(comic_story)" title="The Big Hush (comic story)">
            The Big Hush
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          After Clara accidently freed the
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Djinx?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Djinx (page does not exist)">
           Djinx
          </a>
          from his imprisonment, the Doctor was trapped in his TARDIS by the vengeful entity. Sending Clara instructions on her phone, the Doctor was able to instruct Clara on how to defeat the Djinx and free himself. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Doctor_in_a_Bottle_(comic_story)" title="Doctor in a Bottle (comic story)">
            Doctor in a Bottle
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor and Clara went on a tour of
          <a href="/wiki/Snowcap_University" title="Snowcap University">
           Snowcap University
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">
           Antarctica
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/2048" title="2048">
           2048
          </a>
          . While taking a
          <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">
           helicopter
          </a>
          ride, they learnt that one of the students,
          <a href="/wiki/Polly_Evans" title="Polly Evans">
           Polly Evans
          </a>
          , had stayed behind at the end of term to join the classified
          <a href="/wiki/Project_Sub-Zero" title="Project Sub-Zero">
           Project Sub-Zero
          </a>
          . When another student,
          <a href="/wiki/Quinn_Norton" title="Quinn Norton">
           Quinn Norton
          </a>
          , who also a part of Project Sub-Zero, was killed in a helicopter crash the Doctor and Clara narrowly avoided being on along with Polly's father
          <a href="/wiki/George_Evans" title="George Evans">
           George
          </a>
          , they returned to Snowcap U to investigate. With the help of the
          <a href="/wiki/Spy" title="Spy">
           spy
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Paul_South" title="Paul South">
           Paul South
          </a>
          the Doctor found an ice cavern where the missing students had been experimented on, engineered by Dr
          <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Audley" title="Patricia Audley">
           Patricia Audley
          </a>
          to survive in extreme cold. Paul, along with an splinter of Clara's, Winnie Clarence, released most of the imprisoned humans from captivity.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor transmitted a signal with his sonic causing Dr Audley's animals to go wild. After feigning betrayal of the two, Winnie threw the Doctor the key to free the hybrid subjects from their cells, and saved the Doctor's life by pulling Dr Audley into a vat of liquid
          <a href="/wiki/Ice" title="Ice">
           ice
          </a>
          after Audley pulled a gun on him. Dr Audley was killed, but Winnie survived when she unwittingly had a syringe of Dr Audley's experimental
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Blue_blood?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Blue blood (page does not exist)">
           blue blood
          </a>
          serum injected into her, allowing her to live inside the ice. Clara realised that this meant that not all of the splinters died saving the Doctor, and several of them had lives of their own. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Blood_and_Ice_(comic_story)" title="Blood and Ice (comic story)">
            Blood and Ice
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Undated_events">
           Undated events
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit Undated events section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131126020959/tardis/images/4/44/EyesOfTwelve.jpg">
           <img alt="EyesOfTwelve" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="EyesOfTwelve.jpg" data-image-name="EyesOfTwelve.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131126020959/tardis/images/thumb/4/44/EyesOfTwelve.jpg/180px-EyesOfTwelve.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="EyesOfTwelve" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="EyesOfTwelve.jpg" data-image-name="EyesOfTwelve.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20131126020959/tardis/images/thumb/4/44/EyesOfTwelve.jpg/180px-EyesOfTwelve.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:EyesOfTwelve.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor helps save
            <a href="/wiki/Gallifrey" title="Gallifrey">
             Gallifrey
            </a>
            . (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/The_Day_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Day of the Doctor (TV story)">
              The Day of the Doctor
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <ul>
          <li>
           The Twelfth Doctor helped his previous incarnations place
           <a href="/wiki/Gallifrey" title="Gallifrey">
            Gallifrey
           </a>
           in a
           <a href="/wiki/Pocket_universe" title="Pocket universe">
            pocket universe
           </a>
           at the end of the
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Great_Time_War" title="Last Great Time War">
            Last Great Time War
           </a>
           . (
           <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
            TV
           </a>
           :
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/The_Day_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Day of the Doctor (TV story)">
             The Day of the Doctor
            </a>
           </i>
           ) While its exact timing is not known, it is possible to date this event as occurring before the Doctor's redecoration of his TARDIS, as the piping in the time rotor is blue as he saves Gallifrey, whereas his redecoration of the TARDIS includes changing the piping to orange.
          </li>
         </ul>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Psychological_profile">
           Psychological profile
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit Psychological profile section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">
           Personality
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit Personality section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013003820/tardis/images/5/5d/Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelfth Doctor in light Mummy on the Orient Express" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor in light Mummy on the Orient Express.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013003820/tardis/images/thumb/5/5d/Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelfth Doctor in light Mummy on the Orient Express" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor in light Mummy on the Orient Express.jpg" height="101" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013003820/tardis/images/thumb/5/5d/Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelfth_Doctor_in_light_Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Unfazed by
            <a href="/wiki/Gus" title="Gus">
             Gus
            </a>
            's threats, the Doctor ponders the
            <a href="/wiki/Foretold" title="Foretold">
             Foretold
            </a>
            's modus operandi. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
              Mummy on the Orient Express
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          A cynical man armed with a dry, acerbic wit, a brutal honesty and a lot of internalised anger, the Twelfth Doctor was a radical change from
          <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
           his predecessor
          </a>
          , adopting a less caring and more hostile nature. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flatline" title="Flatline">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was perfectly comfortable with placing his companions in danger if it meant appeasing his curiosity, often leaving them out of the details in his plans, or using them to distract attention away from himself. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, if he believed the situation was too dangerous for them, the Doctor would send his companions to the safety of the TARDIS while staring down the threat alone. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Despite coming across as uncaring, with a complete disregard for social niceties, he would fight to protect those in his care, and he would react with devastation if harm befell them. Such was his reaction to the death of a female
          <a href="/wiki/Tyrannosaurus_rex" title="Tyrannosaurus rex">
           Tyrannosaurus rex
          </a>
          that had been inadvertently dragged through time by the TARDIS. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, for the most part, the Doctor detached and occasionally callous, reacting with indifference during his first encounter with
          <a href="/wiki/Journey_Blue" title="Journey Blue">
           Journey Blue
          </a>
          , who had just lost
          <a href="/wiki/Kai_Blue" title="Kai Blue">
           her brother
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and laughed at
          <a href="/wiki/Orson_Pink" title="Orson Pink">
           Orson Pink
          </a>
          's name, though he apologised for the latter. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor also showed a strong compassionate streak, putting himself in harm's way to save
          <a href="/wiki/Maisie_Pitt" title="Maisie Pitt">
           Maisie Pitt
          </a>
          from the Foretold, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and assisting Clara in finding Danny in the
          <a href="/wiki/Afterlife" title="Afterlife">
           afterlife
          </a>
          , even after she had attempted to blackmail him. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141016211113/tardis/images/0/0d/TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg">
           <img alt="TITAN 12th 1 TheDoctor" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg" data-image-name="TITAN 12th 1 TheDoctor.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141016211113/tardis/images/thumb/0/0d/TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg/180px-TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg" height="117" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="TITAN 12th 1 TheDoctor" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg" data-image-name="TITAN 12th 1 TheDoctor.jpg" height="117" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141016211113/tardis/images/thumb/0/0d/TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg/180px-TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:TITAN_12th_1_TheDoctor.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor compares himself to his predecessor. (
            <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
             COMIC
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
              Terrorformer
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          While he described himself as having had "sophistication and timeless sartorial elegance" restored, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
            Terrorformer
           </a>
          </i>
          ) the Doctor was not above acting childish; requesting a children's menu at
          <a href="/wiki/Mancini%27s_Family_Restaurant" title="Mancini's Family Restaurant">
           Mancini's Family Restaurant
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) sliding down stairs and ladders, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Monsters_of_Coal_Hill_School_(comic_story)" title="The Monsters of Coal Hill School (comic story)">
            The Monsters of Coal Hill School
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) whistling "
          <a href="/wiki/Another_Brick_in_the_Wall" title="Another Brick in the Wall">
           Another Brick in the Wall
          </a>
          " to annoy Clara, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) ecstatically steering
          <a href="/wiki/Santa_Claus" title="Santa Claus">
           Santa Claus
          </a>
          's sleigh, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and bickering with the likes of
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          and Father Christmas. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140904093843/tardis/images/9/96/Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelfth Doctor inside Aristotle" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor inside Aristotle.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140904093843/tardis/images/thumb/9/96/Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelfth Doctor inside Aristotle" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg" data-image-name="Twelfth Doctor inside Aristotle.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140904093843/tardis/images/thumb/9/96/Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg/180px-Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelfth_Doctor_inside_Aristotle.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor's more wistful side manifests as he turns down
            <a href="/wiki/Journey_Blue" title="Journey Blue">
             Journey Blue
            </a>
            .  (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
              Into the Dalek
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The Twelfth Doctor showed even less restraint than his predecessor, and would get frank and physical with his enemies. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, he had a conflicted sense of morality and struggled with his inner darkness. While he sometimes voiced preconceptions about the
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
           Daleks
          </a>
          or
          <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">
           human
          </a>
          nature, he often questioned his own judgement afterwards. Indeed, behind his cold exterior was a man who was extremely self-reflective, to the point where he questioned whether he was still a good man. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ) The Doctor was well aware of the fact that he often found himself in situations that forced him to make terrible decisions, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and believed he was overbearing, manipulative and consciously aware of his own intelligence. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Eventually, he came to the conclusion that he was neither a good nor bad man, but rather just "an idiot, with a box and a screwdriver. Just passing through, helping out, learning." (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Though he retained a respect for humanity, the Doctor would insult humans for being slow minded and violent, dubbing
          <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">
           Earth
          </a>
          the "planet of the pudding-brains." (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Nonetheless, he tolerated the company of those who could engage him intellectually, as with
          <a href="/wiki/Perkins_(Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express)" title="Perkins (Mummy on the Orient Express)">
           Perkins
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Osgood" title="Osgood">
           Osgood
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and claimed to respect humanity enough to allow it to determine its own future without any interference from him. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ) As with his previous incarnation, the Twelfth Doctor also liked people who got straight to the point, and thought that anyone who wasn't scared in life-threatening situations was an idiot. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Though he did not know the reason, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Blood_Cell_(novel)" title="The Blood Cell (novel)">
            The Blood Cell
           </a>
          </i>
          ) the Doctor expressed a strong dislike for soldiers, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) though retained a respect for
          <a href="/wiki/Alistair_Gordon_Lethbridge-Stewart" title="Alistair Gordon Lethbridge-Stewart">
           the Brigadier
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was also easily annoyed by swashbucklers who did not take things seriously. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He also claimed to dislike liver,
          <a href="/wiki/Karaoke" title="Karaoke">
           karaoke
          </a>
          , mime,
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Babysitter" title="Babysitter">
           babysitters
          </a>
          , bantering, salutes, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) being taken prisoner, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
            Terrorformer
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and
          <a href="/wiki/Pantomime" title="Pantomime">
           pantomime
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Behind_You_(short_story)" title="Behind You (short story)">
            Behind You
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He did, however, like "a show-stopping entrance", (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
            Terrorformer
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and
          <a href="/wiki/Candy_floss" title="Candy floss">
           candy floss
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/All_the_Empty_Towers_(short_story)" title="All the Empty Towers (short story)">
            All the Empty Towers
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140830140858/tardis/images/0/08/Awkward_Hug.jpg">

           <noscript>
            <img alt="Awkward Hug" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Awkward_Hug.jpg" data-image-name="Awkward Hug.jpg" height="102" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140830140858/tardis/images/thumb/0/08/Awkward_Hug.jpg/180px-Awkward_Hug.jpg" width="180"/>

          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Awkward_Hug.jpg">

            The Doctor decides hugging isn't for him.  (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">

            <i>
