          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Unlike his immediate predecessor, the twelfth incarnation was not an affectionate individual, failing to return Clara's hugs, or protesting against them, believing they were just another way to hide one's face, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and also disliked holding hands with others. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was momentarily dumbfounded when
          <a href="/wiki/Maid_Marian" title="Maid Marian">
           Maid Marian
          </a>
          pecked him on the cheek in gratitude for saving her, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and reacted with horror after he was snogged by
          <a href="/wiki/The_Master#As_Missy" title="The Master">
           Missy
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, in a moment of excitement, he kissed Clara's forehead while complimenting her brilliance, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Big_Hush_(comic_story)" title="The Big Hush (comic story)">
            The Big Hush
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and also gave
          <a href="/wiki/Meghan_(All_the_Empty_Towers)" title="Meghan (All the Empty Towers)">
           Meghan
          </a>
          , a donkey he had befriended, a kiss on the head when he thought no one was looking. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/All_the_Empty_Towers_(short_story)" title="All the Empty Towers (short story)">
            All the Empty Towers
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140824012155/tardis/images/1/13/Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg">
           <img alt="Deep Breath story image" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg" data-image-name="Deep Breath story image.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140824012155/tardis/images/thumb/1/13/Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg/180px-Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg" height="94" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Deep Breath story image" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg" data-image-name="Deep Breath story image.jpg" height="94" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140824012155/tardis/images/thumb/1/13/Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg/180px-Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Deep_Breath_story_image.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor's piercing glare. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
              Deep Breath
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Though he initially stated that murder was against his moral code, the Doctor showed a willingness to kill the
          <a href="/wiki/Half-Face_Man" title="Half-Face Man">
           Half-Face Man
          </a>
          if he had to, though with some reluctance, first offering him a drink of alcohol and trying to persuade the clockwork droid to self-destruct of his own free will before engaging in fisticuffs. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He also stated that, despite how much he hated him, he had no intention of killing the Architect, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) but was willing to kill
          <a href="/wiki/The_Master#As_Missy" title="The Master">
           theMaster
          </a>
          to spare Clara from doing it. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He also orchestrated the deaths of two
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Kaliratha?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kaliratha (page does not exist)">
           Kaliratha
          </a>
          that were keeping him prisoner by taking them to a point in time prior to their bodies being discovered. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Unlike his immediate predecessor, the Twelfth Doctor was unwilling to alter the
          <a href="/wiki/Web_of_Time" title="Web of Time">
           Web of Time
          </a>
          , believing it was okay to send people to their deaths if history recorded them as deceased, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Crawling_Terror_(novel)" title="The Crawling Terror (novel)">
            The Crawling Terror
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and also refused Clara's request to save
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Danny Pink
          </a>
          from being hit by a car due to it being a part of her timeline, and undoing it would cause a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paradox" title="Paradox">
           paradox
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Much like his
          <a href="/wiki/Seventh_Doctor" title="Seventh Doctor">
           seventh
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/War_Doctor" title="War Doctor">
           war incarnations
          </a>
          , the Twelfth Doctor was heavily inclined to err toward a greater good and was willing to allow a few inevitable deaths if it meant saving the majority. Through this attitude, he acted like a pragmatist that would not hesitate to abandon someone whose fate was already sealed, nor mourn for an ally until his objective had been reached. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, the Doctor was still willing to save people if their deaths were not an immediate inevitability, desperately yelling for people to flee from
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Paul%27s_Cathedral" title="St. Paul's Cathedral">
           St. Paul's Cathedral
          </a>
          when the
          <a href="/wiki/Cyberman_(Mondas)" title="Cyberman (Mondas)">
           Cybermen
          </a>
          began their invasion, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and attempting to save
          <a href="/wiki/Albert_Smithe" title="Albert Smithe">
           Albert Smithe
          </a>
          from the
          <a href="/wiki/Dream_crab" title="Dream crab">
           Dream crabs
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Also like his previous incarnations, he relied on his companions to keep him from succumbing to his darker nature, but, unlike his predecessors, the Twelfth Doctor actively praised them for it, even claiming that
          <a href="/wiki/Clara_Oswald" title="Clara Oswald">
           Clara Oswald
          </a>
          needed a "raise" for dealing with him. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          In stark contrast to his previous incarnations, the Twelfth Doctor was more willingly to leave a situation if he believed he had nothing to contribute; abandoning
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Jason_Clearfield?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jason Clearfield (page does not exist)">
           Jason Clearfield
          </a>
          when he could not offer medical assistance, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Crawling_Terror_(novel)" title="The Crawling Terror (novel)">
            The Crawling Terror
           </a>
          </i>
          ) abandoning soldiers dying of diseases after solving the mystery of their source, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Silver_Mosquitos_(short_story)" title="Silver Mosquitos (short story)">
            Silver Mosquitos
           </a>
          </i>
          ) leaving Clara,
          <a href="/wiki/Courtney_Woods" title="Courtney Woods">
           Courtney Woods
          </a>
          and Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Lundvik" title="Lundvik">
           Lundvik
          </a>
          to decide the fate of the Moon when he felt it wasn't his place to decide for them, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and leaving the
          <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">
           North Pole
          </a>
          base immediately after defeating the
          <a href="/wiki/Dream_crab" title="Dream crab">
           Dream crabs
          </a>
          , despite Clara claiming the team was still in danger. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) The Doctor justified his attitude by pointing out the dangers of everyday life, claiming that "[everything is] dangerous if you want it to be", and once pointing out to Clara that he was not humanity's mother. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          By his own testament, the Twelfth Doctor did not suffer fools gladly, (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Blood_Cell_(novel)" title="The Blood Cell (novel)">
            The Blood Cell
           </a>
          </i>
          ) nor did he tolerate poor manners, even when held at gunpoint, and he believed that one should make requests politely, as well as avoid bad language. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Despite his grumpy nature, the Doctor got along well with children, giving
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Rupert Pink
          </a>
          an enthusiastic pep talk about fear being a super power, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and comparing the TARDIS' dimensions to the sugar in a coke bottle for
          <a href="/wiki/Maebh_Arden" title="Maebh Arden">
           Maebh Arden
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night" title="In the Forest of the Night">
            In the Forest of the Night
           </a>
          </i>
          ) After realising he had hurt
          <a href="/wiki/Courtney_Woods" title="Courtney Woods">
           Courtney Woods
          </a>
          's feelings, he decided to take her and Clara to
          <a href="/wiki/The_Moon" title="The Moon">
           the Moon
          </a>
          , so that Courtney could be the first girl on the Moon, to help her feel special. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          An absent minded incarnation, the Twelfth Doctor had trouble recognising people's age group, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon" title="Kill the Moon">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) often neglected to ask for people's names because they "weren't his area", (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night" title="In the Forest of the Night">
            In the Forest of the Night
           </a>
          </i>
          ) believed that minor clothing changes hid his identity, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and failed to understand Dr.
          <a href="/wiki/Chang_(Dark_Water)" title="Chang (Dark Water)">
           Chang
          </a>
          's joke about the application of
          <a href="/wiki/Dark_water" title="Dark water">
           dark water
          </a>
          in public swimming pools. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Twelfth Doctor's hatred toward the
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek" title="Dalek">
           Dalek
          </a>
          species was rigid, with Clara describing it as "prejudice". He seemed conditioned to believe Daleks could not change and was closed-minded as he dealt with their presence. After his act of fixing a
          <a href="/wiki/Rusty" title="Rusty">
           malfunctioning "good" Dalek
          </a>
          caused it to revert to "evil," the Doctor was almost pleased that his belief of there being "no such thing as a good Dalek" was vindicated. This horrified Clara, who became angered to the point of slapping him. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek_(TV_story)" title="Into the Dalek (TV story)">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Additionally, the Twelfth Doctor was, at times, critical of his previous incarnations' clothing; thinking that his
          <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Doctor" title="Fourth Doctor">
           fourth incarnation
          </a>
          's
          <a href="/wiki/The_Doctor%27s_scarf" title="The Doctor's scarf">
           scarf
          </a>
          "looked stupid", (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and regarded his immediate predecessor's fondness for
          <a href="/wiki/Bow_tie" title="Bow tie">
           bow ties
          </a>
          as "a bit embarrassing", (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) but complimented Osgood's bow tie as "nice". (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          ) According to
          <a href="/wiki/Affinity" title="Affinity">
           Affinity
          </a>
          , the Doctor kept his predecessors "lodged in his head", and held a low opinion of them and himself. (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Silhouette_(novel)" title="Silhouette (novel)">
            Silhouette
           </a>
          </i>
          ) However, upon seeing
          <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Davies" title="Adrian Davies">
           Adrian Davies
          </a>
          , a teacher at
          <a href="/wiki/Coal_Hill_School" title="Coal Hill School">
           Coal Hill School
          </a>
          with a resemblance to his previous incarnation, the Doctor, mistaking Adrian as Clara's boyfriend, arrogantly assumed that Clara was dating Adrian because of his uncanny resemblance to "a certain dashing young time traveller", reflecting more favourably to his predecessor. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Much as his
          <a href="/wiki/Tenth_Doctor" title="Tenth Doctor">
           tenth incarnation
          </a>
          expressed, the Twelfth Doctor associated
          <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">
           regeneration
          </a>
          with death, recalling
          <a href="/wiki/Snowcap" title="Snowcap">
           Snowcap
          </a>
          as "the place where
          <a href="/wiki/First_Doctor" title="First Doctor">
           he
          </a>
          died". He viewed the process as "huge, [and] terrible", with his self-preservation preventing his memories of the experience from consuming him. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Blood_and_Ice_(comic_story)" title="Blood and Ice (comic story)">
            Blood and Ice
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He also believed that regeneration was to be used only when completely necessary, and to use it to fix a broken toe was "a waste of a life". (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Blood_Cell_(novel)" title="The Blood Cell (novel)">
            The Blood Cell
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Habits_and_quirks">
           Habits and quirks
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit Habits and quirks section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Much like his seventh incarnation, the Twelfth Doctor spoke with a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scottish" title="Scottish">
           Scottish
          </a>
          accent, which he took as an entitlement to complain about things,  (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and was often prone to making subtle or climactic boasts. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flatline" title="Flatline">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          When proposing a theory, the Doctor would use words such as "question" or "proposition", and would begin his conclusion with "answer" or "conjecture". After working out the important questions in his head, he waited for others to come to the same conclusion, becoming increasingly annoyed with each wrong question or answer they proposed. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) When in a moment of realisation or thinking intensely, the Doctor would often tell people to "shut up", regardless if anyone else was speaking. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Like the
          <a href="/wiki/Ninth_Doctor" title="Ninth Doctor">
           Ninth Doctor
          </a>
          labelling humanity as "stupid apes", the Twelfth Doctor would call them "pudding brains" when he found them slow-minded or stupid. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flatline" title="Flatline">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor often made puns, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flatline" title="Flatline">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          ) used clever word play, (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Terrorformer_(comic_story)" title="Terrorformer (comic story)">
            Terrorformer
           </a>
          </i>
          ) or quoted classic fairytales. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Eye_of_Torment_(comic_story)" title="The Eye of Torment (comic story)">
            The Eye of Torment
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829145356/tardis/images/2/21/Twelve_Drink.jpg">
           <img alt="Twelve Drink" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Twelve_Drink.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Drink.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829145356/tardis/images/thumb/2/21/Twelve_Drink.jpg/180px-Twelve_Drink.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Twelve Drink" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Twelve_Drink.jpg" data-image-name="Twelve Drink.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829145356/tardis/images/thumb/2/21/Twelve_Drink.jpg/180px-Twelve_Drink.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Twelve_Drink.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor offers
            <a href="/wiki/Half-Face_Man" title="Half-Face Man">
             Half-Face Man
            </a>
            a drink of whisky. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Deep_Breath_(TV_story)" title="Deep Breath (TV story)">
              Deep Breath
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Unlike his first and eleventh incarnations, the Twelfth Doctor had a tolerance for alcoholic beverages. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Much like his
          <a href="/wiki/Third_Doctor" title="Third Doctor">
           third
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Eighth_Doctor" title="Eighth Doctor">
           eighth incarnations
          </a>
          , he took his tea with extra sugar. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Much like his predecessor, the Twelfth Doctor also used hand gestures to extenuate a point, but applied more dedication to his movements, standing firm, while speaking with conviction, though would become more spontaneous when thinking intensely. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor made a habit of assigning nicknames to others, giving them names based on their appearance, by an accessory they carried or by their profession, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) owing to the fact he often chose to forget people, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and would insist on addressing them as their nickname, calling
          <a href="/wiki/Danny_Pink" title="Danny Pink">
           Danny Pink
          </a>
          "PE", despite Danny being a Maths teacher, due to seeing him as more a PE teacher than Maths. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          When not out adventuring, the Doctor could be found jotting down equations and theories on various chalkboards in the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TARDIS_console_room" title="TARDIS console room">
           TARDIS console room
          </a>
          , or on hard surfaces that could bear chalk markings. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor would occasionally offer out
          <a href="/wiki/Jelly_baby" title="Jelly baby">
           jelly babies
          </a>
          in a similar way to the
          <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Doctor" title="Fourth Doctor">
           Fourth Doctor
          </a>
          , but, unlike his fourth incarnation, the Twelfth Doctor kept his jelly babies in a cigarette case. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Skills">
           Skills
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit Skills section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Highly observant, the Doctor was able to point out the
          <a href="/wiki/Half-Face_Man" title="Half-Face Man">
           Half-Face Man
          </a>
          as non-human from his lack of interest in a burnt dinosaur corpse, and later noticed that he and Clara were trapped in a room full of
          <a href="/wiki/Clockwork_Droid" title="Clockwork Droid">
           Clockwork Droids
          </a>
          because they weren't breathing, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) as well as detecting a light shield aura, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ) finding
          <a href="/wiki/Maebh_Arden" title="Maebh Arden">
           Maebh Arden
          </a>
          's "breadcrumb" trail, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night" title="In the Forest of the Night">
            In the Forest of the Night
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and foiling Clara's attempt to drug him with a
          <a href="/wiki/Mood_drug" title="Mood drug">
           sleep patch
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was also able to make accurate deductions from observing his surroundings, identifying the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Aristotle_(spaceship)" title="Aristotle (spaceship)">
            Aristotle
           </a>
          </i>
          as a medical ship within seconds of being on board, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ) correctly deducing Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Quell" title="Quell">
           Quell
          </a>
          's backstory, and solving the riddle of the
          <a href="/wiki/Foretold" title="Foretold">
           Foretold
          </a>
          within sixty-six seconds. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The twelfth incarnation retained
          <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
           predecessor
          </a>
          's ability to converse with other species, such as
          <a href="/wiki/Dinosaur" title="Dinosaur">
           dinosaurs
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">
           horses
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and
          <a href="/wiki/Donkey" title="Donkey">
           donkeys
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/All_the_Empty_Towers_(short_story)" title="All the Empty Towers (short story)">
            All the Empty Towers
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Much like his
          <a href="/wiki/Tenth_Doctor" title="Tenth Doctor">
           tenth incarnation
          </a>
          , the Doctor also had a good sense of smell, which he used to assess his surroundings to deduce the time period he was in. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Strong and durable, the Doctor was able to support his own weight single-handedly, wrestle the Half-Face Man into a corner, fall out of a high tree branch and shake off the fall quickly, and dive off a bridge into the Thames to swim across the river without being hampered, though the latter two events can be linked to him still being within the early hours of his regeneration, when his physical skills tend to be somewhat exaggerated. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) At a later date, he smashed up the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TARDIS_console" title="TARDIS console">
           TARDIS console
          </a>
          with his bare hands in a grief-stricken rage after learning that Gallifrey was still lost. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_in_Heaven" title="Death in Heaven">
            Death in Heaven
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Like several of his predecessors, the Twelfth Doctor was a highly proficient swordsman, able to best
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          in a duel using a spoon, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ) 
and take on
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Kali?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kali (page does not exist)">
           Kali
          </a>
          's three swords with a single blade. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was also skilled in
          <a href="/wiki/Venusian_aikido" title="Venusian aikido">
           Venusian aikido
          </a>
          , using it to defend himself from
          <a class="new" href="/wiki/Abesse?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Abesse (page does not exist)">
           Abesse
          </a>
          and disarming a distracted
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/PROSE" title="PROSE">
           PROSE
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Blood_Cell_(novel)" title="The Blood Cell (novel)">
            The Blood Cell
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Even without his Venusian aikido, the Doctor proved to be skilled in unarmed combat. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Despite initially forgetting how to pilot his TARDIS due to post-regenerative trauma, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Doctor" title="The Time of the Doctor">
            The Time of the Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          ) the Doctor soon mastered his way around the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TARDIS_console" title="TARDIS console">
           TARDIS console
          </a>
          , being able to save
          <a href="/wiki/Journey_Blue" title="Journey Blue">
           Journey Blue
          </a>
          by piloting the TARDIS around her, one second before her ship exploded. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Like his previous incarnations, the Twelfth Doctor also displayed telepathic abilities, being able to link his mind with
          <a href="/wiki/Rusty" title="Rusty">
           Rusty
          </a>
          to try and show the Dalek the beauty of the universe, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ) put
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rupert_Pink" title="Rupert Pink">
           Rupert Pink
          </a>
          to sleep by placing his index finger on his forehead, editing his memories while he did so, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ) putting Clara through a telepathic scenario with the aid of a
          <a href="/wiki/Mood_drug" title="Mood drug">
           sleep patch
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dark_Water_(TV_story)" title="Dark Water (TV story)">
            Dark Water
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and sending messages on blackboards to Clara while a
          <a href="/wiki/Dream_crab" title="Dream crab">
           Dream crab
          </a>
          was sedating her. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          A credited escapologist, the Doctor boasted at teaching
          <a href="/wiki/Harry_Houdini" title="Harry Houdini">
           Harry Houdini
          </a>
          "everything he [knew]". (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor was a very good gambler, winning $800,000 in less than an hour. He credited his achievement to simple mathematics. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Gangland_(comic_story)" title="Gangland (comic story)">
            Gangland
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          As cunning as his seventh incarnation, the Doctor was able to spin a fatal outcome into an advantage, such as using
          <a href="/wiki/Ross_(Into_the_Dalek)" title="Ross (Into the Dalek)">
           Ross
          </a>
          's death to help him, Clara, Journey and
          <a href="/wiki/Gretchen_Carlisle" title="Gretchen Carlisle">
           Gretchen Carlisle
          </a>
          escape
          <a href="/wiki/Dalek_antibody" title="Dalek antibody">
           Rusty's antibodies
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ) or using the deaths of
          <a href="/wiki/Emile_Moorhouse" title="Emile Moorhouse">
           Emile Moorhouse
          </a>
          and Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Quell" title="Quell">
           Quell
          </a>
          as an opportunity to figure out a way to defeat the
          <a href="/wiki/Foretold" title="Foretold">
           Foretold
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was also able to organise a bank heist to save the
          <a href="/wiki/The_Teller_(Time_Heist)" title="The Teller (Time Heist)">
           the Teller
          </a>
          and its mate, even erasing his planning of the heist to guarantee success. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">
           Appearance
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit Appearance section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          While his predecessors began their lives looking young, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Parting_of_the_Ways_(TV_story)" title="The Parting of the Ways (TV story)">
            The Parting of the Ways
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_End_of_Time_(TV_story)" title="The End of Time (TV story)">
            The End of Time
           </a>
          </i>
          ) the Twelfth Doctor started out appearing very much older. He had short grey hair, a hooked nose and sharp silvery blue eyes, with big ears. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Time of the Doctor (TV story)">
            The Time of the Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He was of a light build. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Chime_Time_(comic_story)" title="Chime Time (comic story)">
            Chime Time
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Most changed were his eyebrows, which went from "delicate" (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Time of the Doctor (TV story)">
            The Time of the Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          ) to extremely thick and furrowed. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Day_of_the_Doctor_(TV_story)" title="The Day of the Doctor (TV story)">
            The Day of the Doctor
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Startled by the change, the Doctor described them as "attack eyebrows", which could "take bottle tops off" and were "ready to set up their own independent state of eyebrows". (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Deep_Breath_(TV_story)" title="Deep Breath (TV story)">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) He later considered his intimidating eyebrows as both a major contributor to his gravitas, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) and the reason many viewed him as a hostile. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/The_Swords_of_Kali_(comic_story)" title="The Swords of Kali (comic story)">
            The Swords of Kali
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Tall and gaunt, he was once described by Clara as looking like a "grey-haired stick insect", (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Listen_(TV_story)" title="Listen (TV story)">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ) with
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          describing him as "pale as
          <a href="/wiki/Milk" title="Milk">
           milk
          </a>
          ". (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood_(TV_story)" title="Robot of Sherwood (TV story)">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          )
          <a href="/wiki/Shona_McCullough" title="Shona McCullough">
           Shona McCullough
          </a>
          described him as a "skeleton man". (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Physically, he resembled
          <a href="/wiki/Lobus_Caecilius" title="Lobus Caecilius">
           Lobus Caecilius
          </a>
          , a man he had met in his
          <a href="/wiki/Tenth_Doctor" title="Tenth Doctor">
           tenth incarnation
          </a>
          , (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Fires_of_Pompeii" title="The Fires of Pompeii">
            The Fires of Pompeii
           </a>
          </i>
          ) with the Doctor himself noting that he had "seen [his] face somewhere before". (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Clothing">
           Clothing
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit Clothing section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829004404/tardis/images/9/9f/The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg">
           <img alt="The Doctor&#039;s New Look" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg" data-image-name="The Doctor's New Look.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829004404/tardis/images/thumb/9/9f/The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg/180px-The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg" height="102" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="The Doctor&#039;s New Look" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg" data-image-name="The Doctor's New Look.jpg" height="102" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20140829004404/tardis/images/thumb/9/9f/The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg/180px-The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:The_Doctor%27s_New_Look.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor shows off his new look to Clara, inside his refurbished TARDIS. (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
              Deep Breath
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Immediately following his regeneration, the Doctor initially wore his predecessor's attire, a Victorian nightshirt, and then a coat that he "bought" from a tramp, before stealing a Clockwork Droid's suit in order to masquerade as one. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) After having a chance to return to the TARDIS, though, the Doctor chose a new outfit for himself, with the intention of "aiming for minimalism", but instead felt that he "came out with magician" after solidifying his wardrobe. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          The Doctor initially donned a navy blue Crombie coat and cardigan with a white collared shirt, matching blue trousers, and black brogue boots. Over the top, he sported a thigh-length, dark blue jacket with red lining, often wearing it with the top button done. On his left hand ring finger, he had a pair of gold rings, a normal gold band and a second ring with a greenish amber setting that rested atop the first band. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Breath" title="Deep Breath">
            Deep Breath
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Occasionally, the Doctor would replace his cardigan with a waistcoat, with colours ranging in dark blue and plain black. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Into_the_Dalek" title="Into the Dalek">
            Into the Dalek
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flatline" title="Flatline">
            Flatline
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Though his Crombie coat remained a constant staple of his appearance, the Doctor would wear variations of his attire, switching from vested garments with a white collared shirt for simply a dress shirt on its own, such as purple, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robot_of_Sherwood" title="Robot of Sherwood">
            Robot of Sherwood
           </a>
          </i>
          ) dark blue, (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Time_Heist" title="Time Heist">
            Time Heist
           </a>
          </i>
          ) or black with a white polka dot pattern. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Kill_the_Moon_(TV_story)" title="Kill the Moon (TV story)">
            Kill the Moon
           </a>
          </i>
          )  Other times, he would dispense with the shirt as well and don a black crew neck jumper with small holes on the front. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Listen" title="Listen">
            Listen
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          ,
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/In_the_Forest_of_the_Night" title="In the Forest of the Night">
            In the Forest of the Night
           </a>
          </i>
          ) On at least one occasion, he also wore a black hooded top over this shirt. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Last_Christmas_(TV_story)" title="Last Christmas (TV story)">
            Last Christmas
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          When going into "deep cover" as
          <a href="/wiki/Coal_Hill_School" title="Coal Hill School">
           Coal Hill School
          </a>
          's temporary caretaker, the Doctor donned a ocher brown warehouse coat over his black crew neck jumper. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Caretaker" title="The Caretaker">
            The Caretaker
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141012134908/tardis/images/4/46/Orient_dress.jpg">
           <img alt="Orient dress" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Orient_dress.jpg" data-image-name="Orient dress.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141012134908/tardis/images/thumb/4/46/Orient_dress.jpg/180px-Orient_dress.jpg" height="93" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Orient dress" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Orient_dress.jpg" data-image-name="Orient dress.jpg" height="93" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141012134908/tardis/images/thumb/4/46/Orient_dress.jpg/180px-Orient_dress.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Orient_dress.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Doctor and Clara dress formally for a journey aboard the
            <a href="/wiki/Orient_Express_(spacecraft)" title="Orient Express (spacecraft)">
             Orient Express
            </a>
            . (
            <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
             TV
            </a>
            :
            <i>
             <a href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express_(TV_story)" title="Mummy on the Orient Express (TV story)">
              Mummy on the Orient Express
             </a>
            </i>
            )
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          While aboard the spacecraft
          <a href="/wiki/Orient_Express_(spacecraft)" title="Orient Express (spacecraft)">
           Orient Express
          </a>
          , the Doctor wore a very formal attire consisting of a black double-breasted evening jacket, black trousers, grey waistcoat, his black brogue boots, a white dress shirt and a black cravat. (
          <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
           TV
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mummy_on_the_Orient_Express" title="Mummy on the Orient Express">
            Mummy on the Orient Express
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          While visiting
          <a href="/wiki/1963" title="1963">
           1963
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas" title="Las Vegas">
           Las Vegas
          </a>
          , the Doctor donned a blue
          <a href="/wiki/Fedora" title="Fedora">
           Fedora
          </a>
          at Clara's urging. (
          <a href="/wiki/COMIC" title="COMIC">
           COMIC
          </a>
          :
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Gangland_(comic_story)" title="Gangland (comic story)">
            Gangland
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">
           Behind the scenes
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Twelfth_Doctor?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit Behind the scenes section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Like the
           <a href="/wiki/War_Doctor" title="War Doctor">
            War
           </a>
           and
           <a href="/wiki/Ninth_Doctor" title="Ninth Doctor">
            Ninth Doctors
           </a>
           , the Twelfth Doctor debuted on television before his
           <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">
            regeneration
           </a>
           from his predecessor was screened.
          </li>
          <li>
           His first words  "Kidneys! I've got new kidneys!"  keep to the modern tradition of new Doctors commenting on their bodies. Previously, the
           <a href="/wiki/Ninth_Doctor" title="Ninth Doctor">
            Ninth Doctor
           </a>
           commented on his ears, (
           <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
            TV
           </a>
           :
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/Rose_(TV_story)" title="Rose (TV story)">
             Rose
            </a>
           </i>
           ) the
           <a href="/wiki/Tenth_Doctor" title="Tenth Doctor">
            Tenth Doctor
           </a>
           commented on his "new
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Teeth" title="Teeth">
            teeth
           </a>
           ", (
           <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
            TV
           </a>
           :
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/The_Parting_of_the_Ways_(TV_story)" title="The Parting of the Ways (TV story)">
             The Parting of the Ways
            </a>
           </i>
           ) and the
           <a href="/wiki/Eleventh_Doctor" title="Eleventh Doctor">
            Eleventh
           </a>
           on his legs. (
           <a href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
            TV
           </a>
           :
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/The_End_of_Time_(TV_story)" title="The End of Time (TV story)">
             The End of Time
            </a>
           </i>
           )
           <ul>
            <li>
             In
             <a href="/wiki/DWM_477" title="DWM 477">
              DWM 477
             </a>
             , showrunner
             <a href="/wiki/Steven_Moffat" title="Steven Moffat">
              Steven Moffat
             </a>
             jokingly answered one fan's question on what colour the Doctor's kidneys now were (he had complained he hated their colour) as "Froon. This is an entirely new colour, which only the Doctor can see."
            </li>
           </ul>
          </li>
          <li>
           His costume was revealed in
           <a href="/wiki/DWM_470" title="DWM 470">
            DWM 470
           </a>
           and online earlier than planned to preempt a tabloid scoop.
          </li>
          <li>
           He starred in
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/The_Daft_Dimension" title="The Daft Dimension">
             The Daft Dimension
            </a>
           </i>
           , a comic strip published in
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/Doctor_Who_Magazine" title="Doctor Who Magazine">
             Doctor Who Magazine
            </a>
           </i>
           .
          </li>
          <li>
           Peter Capaldi wanted to wear his
           <a class="new" href="/wiki/Wedding_ring?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Wedding ring (page does not exist)">
            wedding ring
           </a>
           as part of his Doctor's attire, and requested a prop to disguise it. He was given an amber ring with a gemstone that fits over the top of his original band. The
           <a href="/wiki/First_Doctor" title="First Doctor">
            First Doctor
           </a>
           also wore a gemstone ring, and as such the Twelfth Doctor is the first incarnation since then seen to sport one. He is also the first incarnation since the
           <a href="/wiki/Third_Doctor" title="Third Doctor">
            Third Doctor
           </a>
           to wear an ordinary ring.
           <ul>
            <li>
             Promotional material for
             <i>
              <a href="/wiki/Doctor_Who_Experience_(London/Cardiff)" title="Doctor Who Experience (London/Cardiff)">
               Doctor Who Experience
              </a>
             </i>
             mentions that the green amber stone on the Twelfth Doctor's ring was 'allegedly' collected on the
             <a href="/wiki/Planet" title="Planet">
              planet
             </a>
             <a href="/wiki/Raxacoricofallapatorius" title="Raxacoricofallapatorius">
              Raxacoricofallapatorius
             </a>
             . However, this has yet to be stated in the narrative.
            </li>
           </ul>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <table cellspacing="0" class="navbox" style=";">
